# <a name="troubleshooting-windows-mixed-reality-faqs"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-104">Windows Mixed Reality (常见问题的疑难解答) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-104">Troubleshooting Windows Mixed Reality (FAQs)</span></span>

## <a name="understanding-common-installation-error-messages"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-105">了解常见安装错误消息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-105">Understanding common installation error messages</span></span>

### <a name="your-pc-cant-run-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-106">"你的电脑无法运行 Windows Mixed Reality"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-106">"Your PC can’t run Windows Mixed Reality"</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-107">你的电脑不满足运行 Windows Mixed Reality 所需的 [最低要求](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-107">Your PC doesn’t meet the [minimum requirements](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines) needed to run Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-108">这可能是因为计算机的硬件设置与 Windows Mixed Reality 不兼容，或者你需要 [更新到最新版本的 windows](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/12373/windows-update-faq)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-108">This could be because the computer’s hardware setup isn’t compatible with Windows Mixed Reality, or because you need to [update to the latest version of Windows](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/12373/windows-update-faq).</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="79562-109">请注意，Windows Mixed Reality 需要至少支持 WDDM 2.2 的图形卡驱动程序，因此请确保具有制造商提供的最新驱动程序更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-109">Note that Windows Mixed Reality requires a graphics card driver that supports at least WDDM 2.2, so make sure you have the latest driver update from the manufacturer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-110">如果 Windows Mixed Reality 安装程序显示您的图形卡无法满足要求，而您认为图形卡有问题，请确保将您的耳机插入正确的卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-110">If Windows Mixed Reality setup says your graphics card doesn’t meet the requirements and you think it does, make sure your headset is plugged into the correct card.</span></span>

### <a name="youre-nearly-therethis-pc-doesnt-meet-the-minimum-requirements-needed-to-run-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-111">"您差不多，这台电脑不满足运行 Windows Mixed Reality 所需的最低要求"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-111">"You’re nearly there—this PC doesn’t meet the minimum requirements needed to run Windows Mixed Reality"</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-112">你的 PC 不满足 Windows Mixed Reality 中最佳体验所需的 [最低要求](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-112">Your PC doesn’t meet the [minimum requirements](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines) needed for the best experience in Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-113">你的电脑可能能够运行沉浸式耳机，但可能无法运行某些应用程序，或者可能存在性能问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-113">Your PC may be able to run an immersive headset, but may not be able to run certain applications or might have problems with performance.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-114">请注意，Windows Mixed Reality 需要至少支持 WDDM 2.2 的图形卡驱动程序，因此请确保具有制造商提供的最新驱动程序更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-114">Note that Windows Mixed Reality requires a graphics card driver that supports at least WDDM 2.2, so make sure you have the latest driver update from the manufacturer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-115">如果 Windows Mixed Reality 安装程序显示您的图形卡无法满足要求，而您认为图形卡有问题，请确保将您的耳机插入正确的卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-115">If Windows Mixed Reality setup says your graphics card doesn’t meet the requirements and you think it does, make sure your headset is plugged into the correct card.</span></span>

### <a name="before-we-can-set-up-windows-mixed-reality-your-administrator-will-need-to-enable-it-for-your-organization-learn-more"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-116">"在可以设置 Windows Mixed Reality 之前，管理员将需要为你的组织启用它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-116">"Before we can set up Windows Mixed Reality, your administrator will need to enable it for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-117">了解更多 "</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-117">Learn More"</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-118">你可能在使用企业托管网络，而你的组织正在使用 Windows Server Update Services (WSUS) 或具有可能会阻止下载的其他策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-118">You are probably on an enterprise managed network and your organization is using Windows Server Update Services (WSUS) or has other policies that may block the download.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-119">请联系组织的 IT 部门或系统管理员，以 [启用 Windows Mixed Reality](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/application-management/manage-windows-mixed-reality#enable)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-119">Contact your organization's IT department or system administrator to [enable Windows Mixed Reality](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/application-management/manage-windows-mixed-reality#enable).</span></span>

### <a name="we-couldnt-download-the-mixed-reality-software-or-hang-tight-while-we-do-some-downloading"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-120">"我们无法下载混合现实软件" 或 "在我们进行一些下载时挂起"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-120">"We couldn't download the mixed reality software" or "Hang tight while we do some downloading"</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79562-121">有时挂起的更新可能会阻止混合现实软件下载。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-121">Sometimes a pending update can block the Mixed Reality Software download.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-122">转到 " **设置" > 更新 & 安全 > Windows 更新** ，并确保已打开 "Windows 更新"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-122">Go to **Settings > Update & security > Windows Update** and make sure Windows Update is turned on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-123">然后下载并安装任何等待安装的更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-123">Then download and install any updates that are waiting to be installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-124">如果在尝试执行这些步骤时出现 Windows 更新错误，请转到 [此处](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/10164/fix-windows-update-errors)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-124">If you get an error with Windows Update when attempting these steps go [here](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/10164/fix-windows-update-errors).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-125">请确保你的电脑已连接到 internet，并且至少有2GB 的可用存储空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-125">Make sure your PC is connected to the internet and has at least 2GB of free storage space.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-126">检查网络状态： **设置 > 网络 & Internet > 状态** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-126">Check your network status at: **Settings > Network & Internet > Status** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-127">如果无法连接到 internet，请访问 [此处](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/10741/windows-10-fix-network-connection-issues) 获取帮助。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-127">If you are unable to connect to the internet go [here](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/10741/windows-10-fix-network-connection-issues) for help.</span></span>  
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-128">重启电脑，然后重试。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-128">Restart your PC and try again.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="79562-129">如果先前的解决方案不起作用，请尝试执行以下操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-129">If the previous solutions don't work, try:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-130">如果 Wi-fi 网络连接设置为 " [按流量计费](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/17452/windows-metered-internet-connections-faq)"，请将其更改为 "不按流量"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-130">If your Wi-Fi network connection is set to [metered](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/17452/windows-metered-internet-connections-faq), change it to unmetered.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-131">若要关闭按流量计费的连接，请转到： " **设置" > 网络 & Internet > 状态 > "更改连接属性" > 设置为按流量计费的连接** ，然后选择 "关闭"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-131">To turn off a metered connection, go to: **Settings > Network & Internet > Status > Change connection properties > Set as metered connection** and select "Off".</span></span>  
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-132">如果最近安装了更新，则可能会导致问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-132">If you recently installed an update, it can cause problems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-133">建议您不要删除任何已安装的更新，尤其是安全更新，使您的 PC 保持安全，但有时删除最新的更新可帮助确定问题的根源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-133">We don’t recommend that you remove any installed updates, especially security updates which keep your PC safe, but sometimes removing the most recent update can help determine the source of the problem.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-134">要执行此操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-134">To do this:</span></span> 
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-135">请参阅 " **设置" > 更新 & 安全 > 查看已安装的更新历史记录 > 卸载更新**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-135">Go to **Settings > Update & Security > View Installed Update History > Uninstall Updates**</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-136">选择上次安装的更新，然后选择 "卸载"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-136">Select the last update installed and "Uninstall".</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-137">出现 "是否确实要卸载此更新？" 提示时</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-137">When prompted "Are you sure you want to uninstall this update?"</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-138">回答 "是"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-138">answer "Yes".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-139">如果在尝试执行这些步骤时收到错误，请转到 [此处](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/10164/fix-windows-update-errors)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-139">If you get an error when attempting these steps go [here](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/10164/fix-windows-update-errors).</span></span> 
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-140">重启电脑，然后重试。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-140">Restart your PC and try again.</span></span> 
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-141">如果 Windows Mixed Reality 安装正确，请在 "设置" **> Windows 更新 > 检查更新** ，并查看 Windows mixed reality 是否继续运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-141">If Windows Mixed Reality installs correctly, reinstall the latest updates under **Settings > Windows Update > Check for Updates** and see if Windows Mixed Reality continues to work.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-142">如果未正确安装，请重新安装最新更新，并与 Windows 支持部门联系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-142">If it does not install correctly, reinstall the latest updates and contact Windows Support.</span></span> 

### <a name="something-went-wrong-and-we-couldnt-start-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-143">"出现错误，无法启动 Windows Mixed Reality"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-143">"Something went wrong, and we couldn't start Windows Mixed Reality"</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-144">从电脑拔下耳机电缆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-144">Unplug both cables of your headset from the PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-145">重启电脑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-145">Restart the PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-146">转到 " **设置" > 更新 & 安全 > Windows 更新** ，并确保已打开 "Windows 更新"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-146">Go to **Settings > Update & security > Windows Update** and make sure that Windows Update is turned on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-147">然后下载并安装任何等待更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-147">Then download and install any waiting updates.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-148">将耳机重新连接到电脑，然后重试安装。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-148">Reconnect your headset to the PC and then try setup again.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-149">如果上述步骤不起作用，请尝试卸载然后重新安装 Windows Mixed Reality：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-149">If the above steps don’t work, try uninstalling and then reinstalling Windows Mixed Reality:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-150">**> Mixed reality** 中转到 "设置" > 卸载，然后选择 "卸载"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-150">Go to **Settings > Mixed reality > Uninstall** and select "Uninstall".</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-151">重启你的电脑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-151">Restart your PC.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-152">若要再次开始安装过程，只需将耳机插入 PC 即可。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-152">To start the setup process again, just plug your headset into your PC.</span></span>
    

## <a name="troubleshooting-setup-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-153">安装问题疑难解答</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-153">Troubleshooting setup questions</span></span> 

### <a name="my-xbox-controller-isnt-working-with-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-154">我的 Xbox 控制器不能与 Windows Mixed Reality 一起使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-154">My Xbox controller isn't working with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79562-155">确保控制器已打开、完全充电并连接到 PC。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-155">Make sure your controller is turned on, fully charged, and connected to the PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-156">更换控制器的电池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-156">Replace the controller’s batteries.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-157">如果使用的是蓝牙控制器，请在计算机上的 " **设置" > 设备 "> 蓝牙 & 其他设备** ，并确保其配对 (应在页面) 上列出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-157">If you're using a Bluetooth controller, go to **Settings > Devices > Bluetooth & other devices** on your PC and make sure it's paired (it should be listed on the page).</span></span>

### <a name="i-cant-direct-input-controllers-gamepad-mousekeyboard-into-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-158">我无法将输入 (控制器、游戏板、鼠标/键盘) 连接到 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-158">I can't direct input (controllers, gamepad, mouse/keyboard) into Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-159">在戴戴戴显示设备上时，输入应通过耳机的状态传感器自动切换到混合现实体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-159">When you put on your headset, input should automatically get toggled to your mixed reality experience through your headset's presence sensor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-160">桌面上应显示一个蓝色栏：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-160">A blue bar should appear on your Desktop:</span></span>

![向耳机定向输入的 Windows 桌面](images/1050px-windowsy.png)

<span data-ttu-id="79562-162">如果输入未自动切换，则需要手动切换耳机的输入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-162">If input doesn't get toggled automatically, you will need to manually toggle input to your headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-163">为此，可以在键盘上键入 " **Windows 键 + Y** " (，并将输入切换回桌面) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-163">You can do this by typing **Windows Key + Y** on your keyboard (and the same to toggle input back to the desktop).</span></span>

### <a name="when-i-plug-in-my-headset-nothing-happens-the-mixed-reality-portal-doesnt-open"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-164">接通耳机后，没有任何反应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-164">When I plug in my headset, nothing happens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-165">混合现实门户不会打开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-165">The Mixed Reality Portal doesn’t open.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="79562-166">混合现实门户是指通过 Windows Mixed Reality 安装程序的应用程序，它设计为在你插入兼容的耳机时自动打开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-166">Mixed Reality Portal, the app that takes you through Windows Mixed Reality setup, is designed to open automatically when you plug in a compatible headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-167">如果未打开，请在 "搜索" 框中输入 "混合现实门户"，从此处打开该应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-167">If it doesn’t open, go to Start and type "Mixed Reality Portal" in the Search box to open the app from there.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-168">如果找不到混合现实门户，这可能意味着你需要 [更新到最新版本的 Windows](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/12373/windows-update-faq)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-168">If you can’t find Mixed Reality Portal, that might mean you need to [update to the latest version of Windows](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/12373/windows-update-faq).</span></span>

### <a name="how-do-i-choose-between-seated-and-standing-and-all-experiences"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-169">如何实现在 "固定" 和 "所有体验" 之间进行选择吗？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-169">How do I choose between "Seated and standing" and "All experiences"?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-170">如果在头戴式耳机设置期间或更高版本中选择 "固定和放置"，则将使用头戴式耳机而不使用边界。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-170">If you choose "Seated and standing", either during headset setup or later on, you'll be using your headset without a boundary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-171">您可以坐在那里，但您需要停留在一个地方，因为您没有边界来帮助您避免物理障碍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-171">You can sit down or stand up, but you'll otherwise need to stay in one place, as you’ll have no boundary to help you avoid physical obstacles.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-172">某些应用程序可能会设计为使用边界，因此你可能无法使用这些应用程序，或者如果你在没有边界的情况下使用它们，则可能没有相同的体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-172">Some apps might be designed to work with a boundary, so you might not be able to use them or you might not have the same experience if you use them without a boundary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-173">请参阅 "什么是边界，为什么要创建一个？"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-173">See "What's a boundary and why should I create one?"</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-174">以获取详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-174">below for more information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-175">如果你选择 "所有体验"，你将设置一个边界，你可以使用适用于边界以及不需要的应用和体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-175">If you choose "All experiences", you'll set up a boundary and you can use apps and experiences that work with a boundary as well as those that don't require one.</span></span> 

### <a name="learn-mixed-reality-didnt-run-on-first-launch-and-i-went-right-into-the-windows-mixed-reality-home"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-176">了解混合现实首次启动时未运行，并直接进入 Windows Mixed Reality 主页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-176">Learn Mixed Reality didn't run on first launch, and I went right into the Windows Mixed Reality home.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-177">可以按照 [重新运行步骤](learn-mixed-reality.md#how-do-i-re-run-the-learning-experience)重新运行学习体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-177">You can re-run the learning experience by following the [re-run steps](learn-mixed-reality.md#how-do-i-re-run-the-learning-experience).</span></span> 


## <a name="boundary-setup-and-other-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-178">边界设置和其他问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-178">Boundary setup and other questions</span></span>

### <a name="whats-a-boundary-and-why-should-i-create-one"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-179">什么是边界，为何要创建它？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-179">What's a boundary and why should I create one?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-180">边界定义了在戴上 Windows Mixed Reality 沉浸式耳机时可以移动的区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-180">A boundary defines the area in which you can move around while you're wearing your Windows Mixed Reality immersive headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-181">由于你在使用头戴式耳机时看不到你的环境，因此请务必创建边界以帮助避免障碍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-181">Because you can't see your surroundings while you're using your headset, it's important to create a boundary to help you avoid obstacles.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-182">边界看起来就像混合现实中的白色轮廓，并在接近它时出现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-182">The boundary looks like a white outline inside mixed reality and appears when you come close to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-183">当你看到此情况时，会减慢移动速度，并避免超出边界或扩展粗枝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-183">When you see it, slow your movements, and avoid crossing the boundary or extending your limbs beyond it.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-184">边界内的区域应该无家具、低悬挂光装置、天花板风扇等，因此不会出现任何东西。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-184">The area inside the boundary should be free of furniture, low-hanging light fixtures, ceiling fans, etc. so you won't bump into or trip over anything.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-185">[了解 Windows Mixed Reality 中的运行状况和安全性](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039969/windows-10-mixed-reality-immersive-headset-health-safety-comfort)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-185">[Learn about health and safety in Windows Mixed Reality](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039969/windows-10-mixed-reality-immersive-headset-health-safety-comfort).</span></span>

### <a name="how-do-i-create-a-boundary"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-186">如何实现创建边界？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-186">How do I create a boundary?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-187">首次设置耳机时，安装应用 (混合现实门户) 会指导你完成创建边界的步骤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-187">When you first set up your headset, the setup app (Mixed Reality Portal) will take you through the steps to create a boundary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-188">但你可以随时创建一个。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-188">But you can create one at any time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-189">要执行此操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-189">To do this:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-190">在桌面上选择 " **启动 > 混合现实门户** "。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-190">Select **Start > Mixed Reality Portal** on your desktop.</span></span> 
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-191">打开 "菜单"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-191">Open "Menu".</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-192">选择 "运行安装程序" 以创建新边界。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-192">Select "Run setup" to create a new boundary.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-193">如果其他人使用你的耳机，请确保它们了解边界以及如何使用它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-193">If someone else uses your headset, make sure they understand the boundary and how to use it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-194">如果将耳机移动到新位置，则需要设置一个适用于该空间的新边界。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-194">If you move your headset to a new location, you'll need to set up a new boundary that works for that space.</span></span>

### <a name="i-get-an-error-message-when-i-try-to-create-a-boundary"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-195">尝试创建边界时，收到错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-195">I get an error message when I try to create a boundary.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79562-196">创建边界时，请勿接近墙壁或其他障碍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-196">Don't get too close to a wall or other obstruction when creating a boundary.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-197">请确保在跟踪边界时，将耳机置于 waist 高度，并面对计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-197">Make sure to hold your headset at waist height, and face your computer while you trace the boundary.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-198">请确保传感器未被阻止且有足够的光线。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-198">Make sure the sensor isn’t blocked and there’s enough light.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-199">正在跟踪的空间应大于三个平方米。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-199">The space you’re tracing should be larger than three square meters.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-200">空间不应太大或太复杂。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-200">The space should not be too large or too complicated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-201">坚持使用简单的几何形状，无需太多的旋转。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-201">Stick to a simple geometric shape without a lot of twists and turns.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-202">请不要在跟踪时返回到自己的路径。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-202">Don’t cross back over your own path as you’re tracing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-203">如果你的角落停滞，请重新开始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-203">If you get stuck in a corner, start over.</span></span>

### <a name="during-start-up-of-mixed-reality-im-stuck-at-the-step-turn-your-head-side-to-side-and-then-at-the-floor"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-204">在混合现实的启动过程中，我一直在步骤 "将您的头部转向一边，然后在地面"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-204">During start up of Mixed Reality, I'm stuck at the step "Turn your head side to side, and then at the floor".</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-205">此步骤允许耳机识别空间，并还原任何现有的虚拟楼层和边界。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-205">This step lets your headset recognize your space and restore any existing virtual floor and boundary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-206">当你放在你的耳机上时，此扫描过程可能需要长达10秒的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-206">When you put on your headset, this scanning process can take up to 10 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-207">完成后，你将处于混合现实家里，否则系统将提示你再次设置边界。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-207">After it is complete, you will either be in the Mixed Reality Home or you will be prompted to set up your boundary again.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-208">如果扫描过程所用时间超过10秒，则耳机中的邻近感应传感器可能出现问题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-208">If the scanning process takes longer than 10 seconds, there could be a problem with the proximity sensor in the headset:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-209">检查是否已从邻近感应传感器中删除不干胶标签。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-209">Check that the sticker has been removed from the proximity sensor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-210">邻近感应感应器位于耳机内，大致位于 forehead 的中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-210">The proximity sensor is located inside the headset roughly where the center of your forehead would be.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-211">检查邻近感应传感器是否正在将输入切换到你的耳机：使用手指覆盖并抽出几次近程传感器，验证输入是否正在切换到耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-211">Check that your proximity sensor is toggling input to your headset: with your finger, cover and uncover the proximity sensor a few times to verify input is switching to the headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-212">你应在电脑顶部看到 " **Windows 键 + Y** " 横幅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-212">You should see the **Windows Key + Y** banner at the top of your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-213">您可以通过在键盘上键入 **Windows Key + Y** ，随时手动切换到耳机的输入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-213">You can manually switch input to the headset at any time by typing **Windows Key + Y** on your keyboard.</span></span>

### <a name="i-see-a-message-that-says-my-boundary-cant-be-found-what-should-i-do"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-214">我看到一条消息，指出找不到边界。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-214">I see a message that says my boundary can't be found.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-215">  应采取何种操作？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-215">What should I do?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-216">Windows Mixed Reality 在识别现有边界时可能会遇到问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-216">Windows Mixed Reality might have trouble identifying your existing boundary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-217">你可以创建新边界，也可以在 "已安装" 和 "运行" 模式下使用你的设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-217">You can create a new boundary or you can use your device in "Seated and standing" mode.</span></span> 

### <a name="i-see-a-message-that-says-lost-tracking-or-we-dont-have-a-boundary-for-this-space"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-218">我看到一条消息，显示 "丢失跟踪" 或 "我们没有此空间的边界"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-218">I see a message that says “Lost tracking” or “We don’t have a boundary for this space”.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-219">您必须创建一个新边界。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-219">You must create a new boundary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-220">要执行此操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-220">To do this:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-221">选择 " **开始 > 混合现实门户** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-221">Select **Start > Mixed Reality Portal** .</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-222">选择 "运行安装程序"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-222">Select "Run setup".</span></span>

### <a name="the-boundary-is-always-visible-how-can-i-make-it-go-away"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-223">边界始终可见。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-223">The boundary is always visible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-224">如何使其消失？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-224">How can I make it go away?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-225">当你接近它时，会出现边界。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-225">The boundary appears when you are close to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-226">如果边界包含的任何部分都具有较窄或不规则的形状，则您可能最终会接近它并导致其出现，而不像您所希望的那样。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-226">If your boundary includes any sections that have a narrow or irregular shape, you might end up getting close to it, and causing it to appear, more often than you’d like.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-227">若要解决此问题，请尝试使用更大、更普通的形状再次创建边界。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-227">To fix this, try creating your boundary again using a larger and more regular shape.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-228">要执行此操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-228">To do this:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-229">选择 " **开始 > 混合现实门户** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-229">Select **Start > Mixed Reality Portal** .</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-230">选择 "运行安装程序"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-230">Select "Run setup".</span></span>

### <a name="how-can-i-turn-off-the-boundary-temporarily"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-231">如何暂时关闭边界？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-231">How can I turn off the boundary temporarily?</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79562-232">选择 " **开始 > 混合现实门户** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-232">Select **Start > Mixed Reality Portal** .</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-233">打开 "菜单"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-233">Open "Menu".</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-234">将 "边界" 转换为 "关"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-234">Turn "Boundary" to "Off".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-235">请确保在边界关闭时保持在一个位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-235">Make sure to stay in one place while the boundary is off.</span></span>


## <a name="problems-in-windows-mixed-reality-home"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-236">Windows Mixed Reality 主页中的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-236">Problems in Windows Mixed Reality Home</span></span>

### <a name="my-controllers-arent-showing-in-my-windows-mixed-reality-home"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-237">我的控制器未显示在我的 Windows Mixed Reality 主页中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-237">My controllers aren't showing in my Windows Mixed Reality Home.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-238">请确保控制器具有完全电池并且使用蓝牙正确配对。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-238">Make sure your controllers have full batteries and that they are paired correctly using Bluetooth.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-239">尝试使用 Windows 按钮关闭和打开控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-239">Try powering the controllers off and on using the Windows Button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-240">如果仍然看不到控制器，请尝试配对，然后在 " **设备 > Bluetooth** " 下的 "设置" 菜单中重新配对每个控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-240">If you still cannot see your controllers, try in-pairing and re-pairing each controller in the Settings menu under **Devices > Bluetooth** .</span></span>

### <a name="the-floor-of-my-windows-mixed-reality-home-doesnt-appear-to-be-at-the-correct-height-or-it-is-slanted"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-241">我的 Windows Mixed Reality 主页的底层看起来不是正确的高度或倾斜。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-241">The floor of my Windows Mixed Reality Home doesn't appear to be at the correct height, or it is slanted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-242">选择 " **开始 > 会议室调整** ，一旦将应用置于世界各地就会启动，以便在戴上耳机时进行更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-242">Select **Start > Room Adjustment** which will launch once you place the app in the world, to make changes while wearing your headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-243">在此应用中，你将被定向到使用触摸板 (运动控制器) 或方向板 (游戏板) 调整地面高度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-243">In this app, you will be directed to use the touch pad (motion controller) or direction pad (gamepad) to adjust the floor height.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-244">如果地面正确，请使用 Windows 按钮退出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-244">When the floor feels correct, use the Windows button to exit back to your Home.</span></span>

### <a name="my-headset-has-stopped-tracking"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-245">我的耳机已停止跟踪。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-245">My headset has stopped tracking.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-246">请确保灯亮起，并且没有任何内容阻碍耳机前面的内部跟踪相机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-246">Make sure the lights are on and that there isn't anything obstructing the inside-out tracking cameras on the front of your headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-247">如果跟踪丢失，可能需要几秒钟才能恢复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-247">If tracking is lost, it can take a few seconds to resume.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-248">如果跟踪未恢复，请尝试重新启动 Windows Mixed Reality 门户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-248">If tracking does not resume, try restarting the Windows Mixed Reality Portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-249">有关更多详细信息，请参阅 [跟踪故障排除](tracking.md) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-249">See [Tracking Troubleshooting](tracking.md) for more details.</span></span>

### <a name="i-cant-show-a-preview-of-what-im-seeing-in-my-headset-on-my-desktop-screen"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-250">我无法在我的桌面上显示我在我的耳机上看到的内容的预览。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-250">I can't show a preview of what I'm seeing in my headset on my desktop screen.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-251">混合现实门户在屏幕底部有一个 " **播放** " 按钮，可用于在桌面屏幕上显示您在手机上看到的内容的预览。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-251">Mixed Reality Portal has a **Play** button at the bottom of the screen that allows you to show a preview of what you're seeing in your headset on your desktop's screen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-252">但出于性能原因，此功能仅适用于在 Windows Mixed Reality 上运行的 Pc，超 (90Hz) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-252">But for performance reasons, this feature is only available on PCs running at Windows Mixed Reality Ultra (90Hz).</span></span>

## <a name="headset-connectivity-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-253">耳机连接问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-253">Headset connectivity issues</span></span>

### <a name="my-computer-does-not-have-an-hdmi-port"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-254">计算机没有 HDMI 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-254">My computer does not have an HDMI port.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="79562-255">如果计算机没有 HDMI 端口，但具有 DisplayPort (DP) ，微型 DisplayPort (miniDP) 或 USB 类型 C (USB-c) 端口来输出视频，则可能需要使用 [支持的适配器](recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-255">If your computer does not have an HDMI port but does have a DisplayPort (DP), mini DisplayPort (miniDP) or USB Type-C (USB-C) port for outputting video, you may need to use a [supported adapter](recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs.md).</span></span>

### <a name="can-i-use-usb-or-hdmi-extension-cables-with-windows-mixed-reality-headsets"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-256">能否对 Windows Mixed Reality 耳机使用 USB 或 HDMI 扩展缆线？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-256">Can I use USB or HDMI extension cables with Windows Mixed Reality headsets?</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="79562-257">Windows Mixed Reality 耳机不支持使用 USB 或 HDMI 扩展电缆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-257">Windows Mixed Reality headsets do not officially support the use of USB or HDMI extension cables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-258">使用这些电缆可能会显著影响混合现实体验，因为在计算机的 USB 控制器与混合现实耳机之间产生的信号完整性和总线功率发生变化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-258">Using these cables may significantly impact your Mixed Reality experience because of variances in resulting signal integrity and bus power between your PC's USB controller and the Mixed Reality headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-259">如果头戴式耳机短暂显示蓝屏，然后在使用过程中打开黑色和混合现实门户的重启或完全取消枚举，或者耳机音频在黑色和正确显示器之间闪烁，请尝试使用不带分机线缆的耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-259">If the headset display briefly shows a blue screen and then turn black and Mixed Reality Portal restarts or completely de-enumerates during use, or if the headset audio cuts out or becomes glitchy, or if the headset flickers between black and the correct display, try using your headset without extension cables.</span></span>

### <a name="i-am-getting-a-check-your-display-cable-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-260">我收到 "检查显示电缆" 错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-260">I am getting a "Check your display cable" error.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79562-261">如果使用任何适配器将耳机连接到电脑，请确保它们支持 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-261">If you are using any adapters to connect your headset to your PC, make sure they support Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-262">在将 HMD 连接到适配器之前，还要尝试将适配器连接到 PC。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-262">Also try connecting the adapter to the PC before connecting the HMD to the adapter.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-263">如果你的电脑同时具有集成图形和离散图形，请确保在活动图形卡上使用 HDMI 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-263">If your PC has both integrated and discrete graphics, make sure you're using the HDMI port on your active graphics card.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-264">在某些情况下，这可能意味着需要将电脑显示器连接到非 HDMI 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-264">In some cases, this may mean that you'll need to connect your PC display to a non HDMI port.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-265">如果你的电脑同时具有集成图形和离散图形，并且集成的图形较旧且不支持 Windows Mixed Reality，请尝试禁用集成的 GPU。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-265">If your PC has both integrated and discrete graphics, and the integrated graphics is older and does not support Windows Mixed Reality, try disabling the integrated GPU.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-266">将电脑监视器连接到电脑的 HDMI 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-266">Connect a PC monitor to your PC's HDMI port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-267">请确保图形驱动程序是最新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-267">Make sure your graphics drivers are up to date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-268">直接从 AMD、Nvidia 或 Intel 下载并安装它们，因为它们可能比发布到 Windows 更新的内容新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-268">Download and install the ones from AMD, Nvidia or Intel directly as they will likely be newer than what's published to Windows Update.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-269">请确保已将耳机的 HDMI 电缆插到电脑上的 **hdmi 输出** 端口，而不是端口中的 hdmi 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-269">Make sure that you plugged your headset's HDMI cable into an **HDMI out** port on your PC, not an HDMI in port.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-270">Windows 可能无法检测显示电缆连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-270">Windows may be unable to detect the display cable connection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-271">打开设备管理器，查看耳机是否列在 "监视器" 下面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-271">Open the Device Manager and see if the headset is listed under "Monitors".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-272">否则，请选择 " **操作" > 扫描硬件更改** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-272">If not, select **Action > Scan for hardware changes** .</span></span> 

### <a name="i-see-a-message-that-says-put-on-your-headset-even-though-i-have-my-headset-on"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-273">我看到一条消息，显示 "戴上耳机"，即使我的耳机已打开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-273">I see a message that says "Put on your headset" even though I have my headset on.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-274">当你放在你的耳机上时，Windows Mixed Reality 可能需要几秒钟才能重新加载空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-274">When you put on your headset, Windows Mixed Reality may need a few seconds to reload your space.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-275">如果此消息不会消失，请确保已从邻近感应传感器（位于重用功能区之间的耳机内）中删除了保护标签。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-275">If this message doesn't go away, make sure the protective sticker has been removed from the proximity sensor, which is on the inside of the headset between the lenses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-276">如果这不能解决问题，请与你的耳机制造商联系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-276">If this doesn't resolve the problem, contact your headset manufacturer.</span></span>

### <a name="a-message-says-connect-your-headset-even-though-ive-plugged-in-my-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-277">即使已插入耳机，消息也会显示 "连接耳机"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-277">A message says "Connect your headset" even though I’ve plugged in my headset.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-278">确保将耳机的 USB 和 HDMI 电缆连接到计算机上的正确端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-278">Make sure the headset's USB and HDMI cables are connected to the correct ports on your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-279">下面介绍如何识别正确的端口：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-279">Here is how to identify the correct ports:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-280">USB 3.0 端口有一个特殊的徽标，其中 "SS" 标记 (表示 "SuperSpeed" ) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-280">USB 3.0 ports have a special logo with an "SS" mark (indicating "SuperSpeed").</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-281">端口的内部片通常为蓝色，而旧的 USB 2.0 端口通常在内部为黑色或白色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-281">The port's inside piece is normally blue, whereas older USB 2.0 ports are typically black or white on the inside.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-282">如果计算机有两个 HDMI 端口，请使用连接到图形卡的端口，而不是计算机的主板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-282">If your computer has two HDMI ports, use the one that connects to the graphics card, not the computer's motherboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-283">这并不总是很明显，但不同的端口通常位于计算机上的扩展插槽中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-283">It's not always obvious which is which, though discrete ports are often located in an expansion slot on the computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-284">如果尝试一个端口但它不起作用，请尝试其他端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-284">If you try one port and it doesn't work, try the other.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-285">从耳机拔下并插入 USB 和 HDMI 电缆，确保它们已安全连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-285">Unplug and plug in the USB and HDMI cables from your headset to make sure they are securely connected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-286">插入 USB 电缆时，请不要在插入 USB 电缆期间暂停。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-286">When plugging in the USB cable, try not to pause during insertion of the USB cable.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-287">打开设备管理器并确认你的耳机是否列在 "Mixed Reality 设备" 下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-287">Open Device Manager and confirm that your headset is listed under "Mixed Reality devices".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-288">双击 "Mixed Reality 设备" 下的耳机，并确认设备状态指示 "此设备正常运行"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-288">Double click on your headset under "Mixed Reality devices" and confirm that the device status indicates "This device is working properly".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-289">设备管理器中列出的设备上的黄色感叹号指示连接到电脑的设备所报告的错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-289">Yellow exclamation marks on devices listed in Device Manager indicate errors reported by the devices connected to your PC.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-290">如果在设备管理器中列出了 "Hololens 传感器" 并带有黄色惊叹号，请双击该设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-290">If "Hololens Sensors" is listed with a yellow exclamation mark in Device Manager, double click on the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-291">如果出现 **"代码10：未安装此设备的驱动程序"。此设备没有兼容的驱动程序 "** ，请按照 [说明](headset-connectivity.md#the-headset-driver-did-not-install-automatically-when-i-plugged-in-the-headset) 手动安装耳机驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-291">If you see a **"Code 10: The drivers for this device are not installed. There are no compatible drivers for this device"** , follow the [instructions](headset-connectivity.md#the-headset-driver-did-not-install-automatically-when-i-plugged-in-the-headset) to manually install the headset driver.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-292">如果你在你的电脑上使用多个混合现实耳机，并已在之前手动安装混合现实耳机驱动程序，则在某些情况下，手动驱动程序更新可能仅适用于当时连接的耳机，而不适用于其他耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-292">If you use multiple Mixed Reality headsets on your PC and have manually installed the Mixed Reality headset driver before, in some circumstances the manual driver update may only apply to the headset connected at the time and not to your other headsets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-293">在这种情况下，你将看到 **"代码31：此设备无法正常工作，因为 Windows 无法加载此设备所需的驱动程序"。 (代码 31) 。设备管理器中的 ALPC 消息不再可用 "** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-293">In this case, you'll see **"Code 31: This device is not working properly because Windows cannot load the drivers required for this device. (Code 31). The ALPC message requested is no longer available"** in Device Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-294">在设备管理器中，右键单击 "Mixed Reality 设备" 下的耳机，然后选择 "卸载设备"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-294">In Device Manager, right click on your headset under "Mixed Reality devices", and select "Uninstall device".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-295">选择 "确定" 以确认并拔出并 replug 你的耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-295">Select "OK" to confirm and then unplug and replug your headset.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-296">如果你查看耳机的部分枚举 (一系列 USB 设备枚举，但设备管理器) 中 "Mixed Reality 耳机" 下没有任何内容，请尝试使用外部 USB 3.0 集线器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-296">If you're seeing partial enumeration of the headset (a series of USB devices enumerate, but nothing under "Mixed Reality headsets" in Device Manager), try an externally powered USB 3.0 hub.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="79562-297">请参阅耳机制造商的网站并更新耳机的驱动程序和固件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-297">Go to the headset manufacturer’s website and update the drivers and firmware for your headset.</span></span>
6. <span data-ttu-id="79562-298">将耳机连接到另一台电脑并打开设备管理器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-298">Connect your headset to another PC and open Device Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-299">即使该 PC 与 Windows Mixed Reality 不完全兼容，你也可以查看你的耳机是否枚举。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-299">Even if that PC is not fully compatible with Windows Mixed Reality, you can check to see if your headset enumerates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-300">如果耳机不在多台电脑上枚举，则可能存在硬件问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-300">If your headset does not enumerate on multiple PCs, it could have a hardware issue.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-301">**适用于 Surface 用户的说明：** 较早版本的 Surface Dock 和 Surface Book USB 集线器固件更新软件与混合现实耳机不兼容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-301">**Note for Surface users:** Earlier versions of the Surface Dock and Surface Book USB Hub firmware update software are incompatible with Mixed Reality headsets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-302">如果在 Surface PC 上收到 "连接耳机" 消息，请检查是否有任何设备在设备管理器中报告了 **"代码10：设备无法启动" 错误** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-302">If you get a "Connect your headset" message on a Surface PC, check to see if any devices are reporting a **"Code 10: The device cannot start" error** in Device Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-303">如果是这样，请 [删除冲突的驱动程序](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4032123/kinect-sensor-is-not-recognized-on-a-surface-book)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-303">If so, [remove the conflicting driver](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4032123/kinect-sensor-is-not-recognized-on-a-surface-book).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-304">只需执行此操作一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-304">You should only need to do this once.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-305">**适用于 Windows 10 N 用户的说明：** 如果你的计算机运行的是 Windows 10 N，则在插入混合现实耳机后，会看到 **"代码28：安装类不存在或无效" 设备管理器错误** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-305">**Note for Windows 10 N users:** If your PC is running Windows 10 N, you'll see a **"Code 28: The install class is not present or is invalid" error** in Device Manager after plugging in your Mixed Reality headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-306">Windows Mixed Reality 不支持 N 版本的 Windows 10。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-306">N-editions of Windows 10 are not supported by Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-307">有关详细信息，请按照这些 [说明](troubleshooting-windows-mixed-reality.md#im-getting-a-the-install-class-is-not-present-or-is-invalid-error-in-device-manager) 进行操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-307">Follow these [instructions](troubleshooting-windows-mixed-reality.md#im-getting-a-the-install-class-is-not-present-or-is-invalid-error-in-device-manager) for more information.</span></span>

### <a name="a-message-says-check-your-usb-cable-or-insufficient-usb-speed"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-308">消息显示 "检查 USB 电缆" 或 "USB 速度不足"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-308">A message says "Check your USB cable" or "Insufficient USB speed".</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79562-309">请确保使用的是计算机上受支持的 USB 3.0 端口：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-309">Make sure that you're using a supported USB 3.0 port on your PC:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-310">请确保将耳机的 USB 电缆全部插入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-310">Make sure that your headset's USB cable is plugged in all the way.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-311">运行 [Windows Mixed REALITY PC 检查](https://aka.ms/pccheckapp) 应用，以确保支持你的电脑的 USB 3.0 控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-311">Run the [Windows Mixed Reality PC Check](https://aka.ms/pccheckapp) app to make sure your PC's USB 3.0 controller is supported.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-312">尝试电脑上的其他每个 USB 3.0 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-312">Try each of the other USB 3.0 ports on your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-313">某些电脑具有多个 USB 3.0 控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-313">Some PCs have more than one USB 3.0 controller.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-314">暂时断开连接到电脑的所有 USB 设备，并仅连接耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-314">Temporarily disconnect all of the USB devices attached to your PC, and only connect your headset.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-315">在自定义构建的 Pc 上，即使某个端口可能标记为 USB 3.0 端口，它也可能连接到 USB 2.0 控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-315">On custom-built PCs, even though a port may be marked as a USB 3.0 port, it may be connected to a USB 2.0 controller.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-316">在手机网络连接上，打开设备管理器，找到并单击从耳机枚举的任何设备，然后参阅 **按连接查看 > 设备** "。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-316">With your headset connected, open Device Manager, locate and single click any of the devices enumerated from your headset, then go to **View > Devices by connection** .</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-317">尝试在另一台电脑上戴上耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-317">Try your headset on another PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-318">如果其他 PC 与 Windows Mixed Reality 不完全兼容，请签入设备管理器查看 "USB 速度是否不足" 消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-318">If that other PC is not fully compatible with Windows Mixed Reality, check in Device Manager to see if you see the "insufficient USB speed" message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-319">如果耳机未在多台电脑上正确枚举，则耳机可能出现故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-319">If your headset does not enumerate properly on multiple PCs, your headset could be defective.</span></span>

### <a name="the-mixed-reality-portal-did-not-launch-automatically-after-i-plugged-in-my-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-320">我接通耳机后，混合现实门户未自动启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-320">The Mixed Reality Portal did not launch automatically after I plugged in my headset.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-321">可能由于根本问题而无法正确检测到耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-321">The headset might not have been detected properly because of an underlying issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-322">尝试手动启动混合现实门户，并查找显示的任何错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-322">Try launching the Mixed Reality Portal manually and look for any error messages that appear.</span></span> 

### <a name="my-headset-stopped-working-after-putting-my-pc-to-sleep-in-hibernation-mode-or-when-restarting-my-pc-with-my-headset-attached"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-323">将电脑置于睡眠状态后，耳机停止工作，在休眠模式下，或在重新启动我的电脑时连接到我的耳机时停止工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-323">My headset stopped working after putting my PC to sleep, in hibernation mode, or when restarting my PC with my headset attached.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-324">打开设备管理器并确认你的耳机是否列在 "Mixed Reality 设备" 下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-324">Open Device Manager and confirm that your headset is listed under "Mixed Reality devices".</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-325">双击 "Mixed Reality 设备" 下的耳机，并确认设备状态指示 "此设备正常运行"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-325">Double click on your headset under "Mixed Reality devices" and confirm that the device status indicates "This device is working properly".</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-326">如果出现 "代码 43" 错误，指出设备已停止工作，或者如果你没有在 "Mixed Reality 设备" 下看到你的耳机，请将其拔出，然后在你的耳机的 USB 电缆中拔出和 replug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-326">If you see a "Code 43" error indicating that the device has stopped working, or if you don't see your headset listed under "Mixed Reality devices", unplug and replug in your headset's USB cable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-327">Microsoft 正在调查可能导致此错误的潜在软件/驱动程序互操作性问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-327">Microsoft is investigating a potential software/driver interoperability issue which may result in this error.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-328">此问题会影响少量 Pc，预计会在将来对混合现实耳机驱动程序的更新中得到解决。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-328">This issue affects a small number of PCs, and is expected to be resolved in a future update to the Mixed Reality headset driver.</span></span>

### <a name="my-headset-causes-my-pc-to-generate-a-bug-check-blue-screen-when-i-put-my-pc-to-sleep-or-when-it-is-in-hibernation-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-329">我的耳机会使我的电脑在计算机进入睡眠状态或处于休眠模式时， (蓝屏) 生成 Bug 检查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-329">My headset causes my PC to generate a Bug Check (blue screen) when I put my PC to sleep or when it is in hibernation mode.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-330">Microsoft 正在调查潜在的软件/驱动程序互操作性问题，这可能会导致少量的 Pc 生成 "9F" Bug 检查 (蓝屏) 当电脑进入睡眠状态或连接到耳机时处于休眠模式时）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-330">Microsoft is investigating a potential software/driver interoperability issue which may result in a small number of PCs potentially generating a "9F" Bug Check (blue screen) when the PC is put to sleep or into hibernation mode with the headset attached.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-331">此问题应在以后对混合现实耳机驱动程序的更新中得到解决。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-331">This issue is expected to be resolved in a future update to the Mixed Reality headset driver.</span></span>

### <a name="the-headset-driver-did-not-install-automatically-when-i-plugged-in-the-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-332">接通耳机后，耳机驱动程序未自动安装。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-332">The headset driver did not install automatically when I plugged in the headset.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-333">在新电脑上，或安装有新安装的 Windows 10 副本的电脑上，耳机驱动程序可在其他 Windows 更新后排队，并且可能不会立即安装。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-333">On new PCs, or PCs with a newly installed copy of Windows 10, the headset driver could be queued behind other Windows updates and may not install immediately.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-334">如果有 "N" 版 Windows，则需要切换到 Windows 10 的常规版本，才能使用 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-334">If you have an "N"-edition of Windows, you will need to switch to a regular edition of Windows 10 to use Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-335">手动安装：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-335">To install it manually:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-336">请参阅 **开始 > 设备管理器** 并在 "其他设备" 下查看 "HoloLens 传感器" 设备的 "其他设备"，其中包含黄色感叹号： ![ 设备管理器 HoloLens 传感器的视图](images/hololenssensors.png)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-336">Go to **Start > Device Manager** and look under "Other devices" for a "HoloLens Sensors" device with a yellow exclamation mark: ![View of Device Manager HoloLens Sensors](images/hololenssensors.png)</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-337">右键单击该设备，然后选择 "属性"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-337">Right click on the device and select properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-338">如果设备的属性读取 **此设备的驱动程序未安装 (代码 28)** ，请关闭该窗口，然后继续。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-338">If the device's properties read **The drivers for this device are not installed (Code 28)** , close the window and proceed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-339">如果有另一条消息，请按照本页其余部分的故障排除步骤操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-339">If there is another message, follow troubleshooting steps on the rest of this page.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="79562-340">![设备管理器中的 HoloLens 传感器的代码28](images/code28.png)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-340">![Code 28 of HoloLens Sensors in Device Manager](images/code28.png)</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-341">再次右键单击该设备，然后选择 "更新驱动程序 ..."然后，在设备更新后 "自动搜索更新的驱动程序软件"，你应会在设备管理器： ![ Mixed Reality 设备显示在设备管理器](images/mixedrealitydevices.png)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-341">Right click on the device again and select "Update Drivers..." and then "Search automatically for updated driver software" After the device updates, you should see your headset listed under "Mixed Reality devices" in Device Manager: ![Mixed Reality Device appear in Device Manager](images/mixedrealitydevices.png)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-342">如果手动安装不起作用，或在其他设备下找不到该驱动程序，则可能需要卸载现有的驱动程序，然后重新安装它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-342">If the manual install doesn’t work, or you don't find the driver under Other Devices, then you probably need to uninstall the existing driver and reinstall it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-343">若要执行该操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-343">To do that:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-344">请参阅 **开始 > 设备管理器** 并在 "混合现实设备" 下查看头戴显示设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-344">Go to **Start > Device Manager** and look under "Mixed Reality devices" for your headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-345">设备状态应指示 "设备正常运行"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-345">The device status should indicate that "The device is working properly".</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-346">右键单击该设备，然后选择 "卸载设备"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-346">Right click on the device and select "Uninstall Device".</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-347">在出现的新弹出窗口中，选中复选框 "删除此设备的驱动程序软件"，然后选择 "卸载"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-347">In the new popup that appears, select the check box "Delete the driver software for this device" and then select "Uninstall".</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-348">完成后，拔出电脑的耳机，并重新插回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-348">When that completes, unplug the headset from your PC, and plug it back in.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-349">Windows 更新现在会下载并安装新的驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-349">Windows Update will now download and install a new driver.</span></span>

### <a name="troubleshooting-flowchart"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-350">故障排除流程图</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-350">Troubleshooting flowchart</span></span>

## <a name="mixed-reality-headset-display-problems"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-352">混合现实耳机显示问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-352">Mixed Reality headset display problems</span></span> ##

### <a name="my-headset-displays-are-black"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-353">我的耳机显示为黑色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-353">My headset displays are black.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79562-354">检查您的 PC 性能和稳定性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-354">Check your PC performance and stability:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-355">使用任务管理器查看是否有任何进程支持您的 PC 的 CPU、GPU 和/或磁盘驱动器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-355">Use the Task Manager to see if any processes are maxing out your PC's CPU, GPU, and/or disk drives.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-356">使用事件查看器) 查看 Windows (中的应用程序和系统事件日志，以查看是否有经常崩溃并生成 Windows 错误报告 (WER) 报告的应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-356">Look at the Applications and System Event Logs in Windows (using Event Viewer) to see if you have an app that is frequently crashing and generating Windows Error Reporting (WER) reports.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-357">检查 Windows 更新，确保你的 Windows 版本是最新版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-357">Check Windows Update to make sure your version of Windows is current.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-358">可能需要多次选择 "检查更新"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-358">You may have to select "Check for Updates" multiple times.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-359">检查应用和游戏稳定性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-359">Check app and game stability:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-360">确保你的计算机满足最低系统要求，以运行任何不能正常运行的应用/游戏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-360">Ensure that your PC meets the minimum system requirements to run any app/game that is not performing correctly.</span></span>    
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-361">确保你的 GPU 驱动程序版本是最新版本，并检查新驱动程序是否存在任何新的性能和兼容性问题和回归。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-361">Make sure your GPU driver version is recent, and check for any new performance and compatibility issues and regressions on new drivers.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-362">如果你使用的是 SteamVR 应用和游戏，请确保 SteamVR 和 SteamVR 组件的 Windows Mixed Reality 是最新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-362">If you are using SteamVR apps and games, make sure SteamVR and the Windows Mixed Reality for SteamVR components are up to date.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-363">检查 HDMI 适配器的兼容性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-363">Check HDMI adapter compatibility:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-364">请确保 HDMI 电缆一直处于插入的方向。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-364">Make sure that the HDMI cable is plugged in all the way.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-365">如果使用的是 HDMI 适配器 (例如，微型 DisplayPort to HDMI 适配器) ，请确保它与 Windows Mixed Reality 兼容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-365">If you're using an HDMI adapter (for example, a Mini DisplayPort to HDMI adapter), make sure it is compatible with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-366">适配器必须支持 HDMI 2.0，并且有许多较早的适配器仅支持1080p。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-366">The adapter must support HDMI 2.0, and there are many older adapters that only support 1080p.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-367">请参阅 [Windows Mixed Reality 的推荐适配器](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-367">See [Recommended adapters for Windows Mixed Reality](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs).</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-368">插头顺序很重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-368">Plug order can be important.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-369">在将耳机连接到适配器之前，请将 HDMI 适配器连接到电脑，尤其是在使用 USB 到 HDMI 适配器的情况下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-369">Connect the HDMI adapter to your PC before connecting the headset to the adapter, especially if you're using a USB-C to HDMI adapter.</span></span> 
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-370">如果正在使用，请尝试删除扩展电缆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-370">Try removing extension cables if you are using them.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-371">检查图形卡和驱动程序兼容性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-371">Check graphics card and driver compatibility:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-372">使用 PC 监视器尝试您的 PC 的 HDMI 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-372">Try your PC's HDMI port with a PC monitor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-373">某些 Pc 可能有多个 HDMI 端口，而且并非所有计算机都处于活动状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-373">Some PCs may have more than one HDMI port, and not all of them may be active.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-374">如果你的电脑同时 (iGPU) 和离散图形处理单位 (dGPU) ，则请确保已将其插入 dGPU 的 HDMI 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-374">If your PC has both an integrated graphics processing unit (iGPU) and a discrete graphics processing unit (dGPU), make sure that you are plugged into your dGPU's HDMI port.</span></span><br> ![HDMI 端口](images/HP_HDMI_Ports_s.png)
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-376">仔细检查 GPU 驱动程序版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-376">Double check your GPU driver version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-377">请确保它是最新的，还应注意任何新的性能和兼容性问题以及新驱动程序的回归。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-377">Make sure it's recent, but also pay attention to any new performance and compatibility issues and regressions on brand new drivers.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-378">如果在笔记本电脑上使用混合现实，并且已从图形卡制造商的网站安装了更新的图形驱动程序，请尝试降级到电脑制造商网站上提供的最新图形卡驱动程序，或 Windows 更新上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-378">If you're using Mixed Reality on a laptop and you've installed a newer graphics driver from the graphics card manufacturer's website, try downgrading to the latest graphics card driver provided on your PC manufacturer's website, or on Windows Update.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-379">如果有多台电脑监视器连接到您的 PC，请尝试暂时断开除一台 PC 监视器以外的所有连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-379">If you have multiple PC monitors connected to your PC, try temporarily disconnecting all but one PC monitor.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-380">如果已为电脑监视器设置自定义刷新速率，请尝试暂时还原为标准刷新率，如60Hz。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-380">If you've set a custom refresh rate for your PC monitor, try temporarily reverting to a standard refresh rate, such as 60Hz.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-381">如果最近更改了图形卡而不重新安装 Windows，请检查耳机式监视器是否仍然安装了正确的驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-381">If you've recently changed your graphics card without reinstalling Windows, check that the headset monitor still has the correct driver installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-382">接通耳机后，确认 "Mixed Reality 耳机" 列在设备管理器的 "监视器" 节点下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-382">With your headset plugged in, confirm that "Mixed Reality headset" is listed under the Monitors node in Device Manager.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-383">如果你的电脑具有 Nvidia 图形卡，请确保已禁用 Nvidia 的3D 远景软件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-383">If your PC has an Nvidia graphics card, make sure that Nvidia's 3D Vision software is disabled.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-384">对于某些图形卡 (特别) 的显卡，HDMI 端口可能不支持 HDMI 2.0，或者可能与 Windows Mixed Reality 完全兼容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-384">On some graphics cards (especially older graphics cards), the HDMI port may not support HDMI 2.0 or may not be fully compatible with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-385">请使用[活动的 DisplayPort 1.2 到 HDMI 2.0 适配器](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs)尝试使用图形卡的 DisplayPort 端口</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-385">Please try your graphics card's DisplayPort port by using an [active DisplayPort 1.2 to HDMI 2.0 adapter](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs)</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-386">Hp Omen 电脑（HP 产品编号为 1RJ99EA # 阿尔）具有与 Windows Mixed Reality 不兼容的 HDMI 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-386">HP Omen PCs with HP product number 1RJ99EA#ABU have HDMI ports that are incompatible with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-387">为此，请打开 "HP 支持助手"，将在应用底部列出产品编号。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-387">To look this up, open up the "HP Support Assistant" and the product number will be listed towards the bottom of the app.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-388">如果你的电脑具有 AMD R9 系列图形卡，并且你使用的是 Samsung 混合现实耳机，则需要将头戴显示设备的固件更新为版本1.0.8 或更高版本，以便将你的图形卡的 HDMI 端口与耳机配合使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-388">If your PC has an AMD R9-series graphics card and you're using a Samsung Mixed Reality headset, you'll need to update your headset's firmware to version 1.0.8 or newer in order to use the HDMI port of your graphics card with the headset.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-389">如果使用的是 Surface Book 2，请确保使用的是从 [USB 到 HDMI 适配器的接口](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-389">If you're using a Surface Book 2, please make sure you're using the [Surface USB-C to HDMI adapter](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/recommended-adapters-for-windows-mixed-reality-capable-pcs).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-390">检查混合现实耳机硬件问题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-390">Check for a Mixed Reality headset hardware issue:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-391">若要确认或排除混合现实耳机的硬件问题，请尝试将混合现实耳机连接到另一台 PC。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-391">To confirm or rule out hardware issues with your Mixed Reality headset, try connecting your Mixed Reality headset to another PC.</span></span> 
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-392">首先检查计算机兼容性和安装问题，因为症状非常类似。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-392">Check for PC compatibility and setup issues first, as the symptoms are very similar.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-393">请检查以确保已将 USB 电缆插入 USB 3.0 或更快的端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-393">Check to make sure the USB cable is plugged into a USB 3.0 or faster port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-394">USB 3.0 端口具有 SS () 写入它们的速度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-394">USB 3.0 ports have SS (Super Speed) written next to them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-395">它们通常 (，但并不总是) 彩色蓝色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-395">They are often (but not always) colored blue.</span></span>        

<span data-ttu-id="79562-396">如果有帮助，请参阅下面的耳机黑色屏幕疑难解答流程图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-396">If helpful, consult the headset black screen troubleshooting flow chart below.</span></span>
