### <a name="my-headset-display-occasionally-turns-black-after-some-use"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-398">有些使用后，耳机显示偶尔会变黑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-398">My headset display occasionally turns black after some use.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79562-399">尝试禁用 PC 可能具有的任何 USB 挂起或节能功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-399">Try disabling any USB suspend or power saving features your PC might have.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-400">例如， [usb 选择性挂起](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows-hardware/drivers/usbcon/usb-selective-suspend) 在 Windows 电源选项中，在设备管理器中选择 "允许计算机关闭此设备以节省电源" 设置，并在 PC 的固件中保存任何 usb 节能设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-400">For example, [USB selective suspend](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows-hardware/drivers/usbcon/usb-selective-suspend) in Windows power options, the "Allow the computer to turn off this device to save power" setting in Device Manager, and any USB power saving settings in your PC's firmware.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-401">暂时断开连接到电脑的任何其他 USB 设备和外围设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-401">Temporarily disconnect any other USB devices and peripherals connected to your PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-402">仔细检查 GPU 驱动程序版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-402">Double check your GPU driver version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-403">请确保它是最新的，还应注意任何新的性能和兼容性问题以及新驱动程序的回归。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-403">Make sure it's recent, but also pay attention to any new performance and compatibility issues and regressions on brand new drivers.</span></span>

### <a name="one-of-the-displays-on-my-headset-is-black"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-404">我的耳机上显示的一个显示为黑色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-404">One of the displays on my headset is black.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79562-405">如果使用的是 HDMI 适配器，请确保它支持 HDMI 2.0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-405">If you're using an HDMI adapter, make sure it supports HDMI 2.0.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-406">删除任何可能使用的 USB 和 HDMI 扩展电缆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-406">Remove any USB and HDMI extension cables that you may be using.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-407">请确保您的图形驱动程序是最新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-407">Make sure your graphics driver is up-to-date.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-408">尝试将混合现实耳机置于另一台电脑上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-408">Try the Mixed Reality headset on another PC.</span></span>

### <a name="my-headset-displays-turn-blue-for-a-moment-and-then-mixed-reality-portal-reinitializes"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-409">我的耳机显示暂时为蓝色，然后混合现实门户重新初始化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-409">My headset displays turn blue for a moment, and then Mixed Reality Portal reinitializes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-410">这通常表示你的电脑上偶尔出现 USB 控制器可靠性问题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-410">This typically indicates an occasional USB controller reliability issue on your PC:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-411">请尝试其他 USB 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-411">Try another USB port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-412">你的电脑可能有多个 USB 3.0 控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-412">Your PC may have multiple USB 3.0 controllers.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-413">如果适用) ，请 (删除任何扩展电缆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-413">Remove any extension cables (if applicable).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-414">尝试从您的 PC 中拔出所有其他 USB 设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-414">Try unplugging all other USB devices from your PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-415">尝试将外部驱动的 USB 3.0 集线器连接到您的 PC，并将您的耳机连接到中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-415">Try connecting an externally-powered USB 3.0 hub to your PC, and connecting your headset to the hub.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-416">如果使用的是台式计算机，请考虑购买 USB 3.0 PCIe 卡，将另一个 USB 控制器添加到您的 PC。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-416">If you're using a Desktop PC, consider purchasing a USB 3.0 PCIe card to add another USB controller to your PC.</span></span>

### <a name="my-headset-causes-my-pc-to-hang-or-show-a-black-screen-while-starting-up"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-417">我的耳机使我的 PC 挂起或在启动时显示黑屏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-417">My headset causes my PC to hang or show a black screen while starting up.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-418">在某些电脑上，在打开或重启电脑时，让你的耳机保持接通电源可能会影响其启动过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-418">On some PCs, leaving your headset plugged in before turning on or while rebooting your PC may interfere with its startup process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-419">你的电脑可以选择耳机显示为 "主监视器" 以显示 PC 启动进度，或者可能会阻止其启动并显示 "挂起" 和/或产生报警音错误代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-419">Your PC could select the headset displays as the "primary monitor" to show PC startup progress or it could be prevented from starting up properly and may "hang" and/or produce a beeping error code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-420">此行为很大程度上取决于 PC 制造商和型号，以及/或者图形卡的品牌和型号。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-420">The behavior depends largely on the PC make and model, and/or the make and model of the graphics card.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-421">解决方法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-421">To fix this:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-422">将耳机连接到图形卡上的其他端口 (可能需要使用适配器) 使用其他端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-422">Connect your headset to a different port on your graphics card (you may need to use an adapter to use the other ports).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-423">请确保您的 PC 的 BIOS/UEFI 固件是最新的 (，但如果您喜欢这样做) ，只需更新您的 PC BIOS/UEFI 固件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-423">Make sure your PC's BIOS / UEFI firmware is up-to-date (but only update your PC's BIOS / UEFI firmware if you're comfortable doing so).</span></span>

### <a name="my-pc-or-headset-displays-flicker-flash-or-remain-black-when-using-a-surface-pc"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-424">使用 Surface PC 时，电脑或耳机显示闪烁、闪烁或保持黑屏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-424">My PC or headset displays flicker, flash or remain black when using a Surface PC.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79562-425">请确保使用的是支持 HDMI 2.0 的 HDMI 适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-425">Make sure you're using an HDMI adapter that supports HDMI 2.0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-426">许多老式的 HDMI 适配器仅支持1080p 分辨率，这对于混合现实耳机来说是不够的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-426">Many older HDMI adapters only support 1080p resolution, which is insufficient for Mixed Reality headsets.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-427">请确保您的图形驱动程序是最新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-427">Make sure your graphics driver is up-to-date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-428">除了检查 Windows 更新之外，您可能还希望查看 PC 制造商的网站中是否有更新的图形驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-428">In addition to checking Windows Update, you may wish to check the PC manufacturer's website for an updated graphics driver.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-429">某些 Surface 设备与 Windows Mixed Reality 不兼容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-429">Some Surface devices are incompatible with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-430">了解有关 [Surface 兼容性和要求](windows-mixed-reality-minimum-pc-hardware-compatibility-guidelines.md#windows-mixed-reality-and-surface)的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-430">Learn more about [Surface compatiblity and requirements](windows-mixed-reality-minimum-pc-hardware-compatibility-guidelines.md#windows-mixed-reality-and-surface).</span></span>

### <a name="my-headset-display-doesnt-work-after-i-shut-down-and-do-a-fast-startup"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-431">关机后，我的耳机显示不起作用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-431">My headset display doesn't work after I shut down and do a fast startup.</span></span>

### <a name="my-headset-displays-are-very-choppy-but-mixed-reality-portals-preview-window-appears-fine"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-433">我的耳机显示显得非常断断续续，但混合现实门户的预览窗口显示良好。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-433">My headset displays are very choppy, but Mixed Reality Portal's preview window appears fine.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79562-435">更新图形驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-435">Update your graphics driver.</span></span>

### <a name="im-getting-a-the-install-class-is-not-present-or-is-invalid-error-in-device-manager"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-436">在设备管理器中收到 "安装类不存在或无效" 错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-436">I'm getting a "The install class is not present or is invalid" error in Device Manager.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-437">如果在设备管理器中看到 "HoloLens 传感器" 带有黄色惊叹号，请双击该设备了解更多详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-437">If you see "HoloLens Sensors" with a yellow exclamation mark in Device Manager, double click on the device for additional details.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-438">如果看到一条消息，指出 "未安装此设备的驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-438">If you see a message saying "The drivers for this device are not installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-439"> (代码 28) -安装类不存在或无效 "，这通常是因为你的电脑正在运行 [Windows 10 N](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039813/media-feature-pack-for-windows-10-n-october-2017)。请注意，N 版 Windows 10 不支持 Windows Mixed Reality，你将需要安装非 N 版本的 Windows 10。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-439">(Code 28) -- The install class is not present or is invalid", this is typically because your PC is running [Windows 10 N](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039813/media-feature-pack-for-windows-10-n-october-2017). Please note that N-editions of Windows 10 do not support Windows Mixed Reality, and you'll need to install a non-N version of Windows 10.</span></span>

### <a name="my-wmr-environment-is-jittery-or-stutters-when-i-move-my-head-and-displays-double-vision"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-440">我的 WMR 环境在移动头时出现抖动或 stutters，并显示双重视觉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-440">My WMR environment is jittery or stutters when I move my head and displays double vision.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-441">在具有集成图形和 Nvidia GPU 的便携式计算机上，在一段时间后出现错误，使上一个帧在下一帧之后显示，从而使双愿景在偏航、音调或滚动移动过程中移动的速度更快。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-441">On a laptop with integrated graphics and an Nvidia GPU, an error occurs after a period of time that appears to cause a previous frame to display after the next frame, resulting in double vision the faster you move your head in a yaw, pitch, or roll movement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-442">此问题似乎出现在 Nvidia 图形驱动程序436.48 之后的驱动程序中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-442">The issue appears to be on drivers after Nvidia Graphics Driver 436.48.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="79562-443">安装此驱动程序将解决此问题，直至 Nvidia 解决更新的驱动程序中的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-443">Installing this driver will fix the issue until Nvidia solves the problem in the updated drivers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-444">若要直接安装 Nvidia 图形驱动程序436.48，请访问 [nvidia](https://www.nvidia.com/Download/driverResults.aspx/152007/en-us)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-444">For a direct install of Nvidia Graphics Driver 436.48, visit [NVIDIA](https://www.nvidia.com/Download/driverResults.aspx/152007/en-us).</span></span>

### <a name="im-experiencing-discomfort-when-i-use-my-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-445">我使用耳机时遇到 discomfort。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-445">I’m experiencing discomfort when I use my headset.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="79562-446">有关 Windows Mixed Reality 中舒适的一般信息，请参阅 [Windows Mixed reality 沉浸式耳机运行状况、安全和舒适](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039969/windows-10-mixed-reality-immersive-headset-health-safety-comfort)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-446">For general info about comfort in Windows Mixed Reality, see [Windows Mixed Reality immersive headset health, safety, and comfort](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039969/windows-10-mixed-reality-immersive-headset-health-safety-comfort).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-447">有关特定耳机的详细信息，请与耳机制造商联系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-447">For details about your specific headset, check with the headset manufacturer.</span></span>

### <a name="how-can-i-get-a-clearer-view-in-my-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-448">如何在我的耳机中获得更清晰的视图？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-448">How can I get a clearer view in my headset?</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="79562-449">尝试调整耳机大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-449">Try adjusting the fit of your headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-450">通过向上、向下或向左和向右移动，调整传送带的位置，并调整传送带，使其感觉 snug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-450">Adjust its position on your face by moving it up and down or left and right, and adjust the straps so it feels snug.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-451">如果耳机支持，还可以调整其校准设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-451">If your headset supports it, you can also adjust its calibration settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-452">如果头戴式耳机有调整校准的旋钮，请使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-452">If the headset has a knob to adjust calibration, use that.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-453">如果没有，请参阅 " **设置" > 混合现实 > 视觉质量** 并调整其中的校准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-453">If it doesn’t, go to **Settings > Mixed reality > Visual quality** and adjust the calibration there.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-454">有关特定设备的校准的详细信息，请与耳机制造商联系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-454">For more information on calibration for your specific device, check with your headset manufacturer.</span></span>

## <a name="mixed-reality-portal-error-messages-and-problems"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-455">混合现实门户错误消息和问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-455">Mixed Reality Portal error messages and problems</span></span>

### <a name="i-got-a-something-went-wrong-error-message-or-im-having-problems-in-the-mixed-reality-portal"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-456">我收到 "出现错误" 的错误消息，或在混合现实门户中遇到问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-456">I got a "Something went wrong" error message, or I'm having problems in the Mixed Reality Portal.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-457">重启 Windows Mixed Reality：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-457">Restart Windows Mixed Reality:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-458">从电脑拔下耳机电缆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-458">Disconnect both headset cables from your PC.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-459">重启你的电脑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-459">Restart your PC.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-460">重新连接耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-460">Reconnect your headset.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-461">如果这不起作用，请确保电脑识别你的耳机：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-461">If that doesn't work, make sure that your PC recognizes your headset:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-462">选择“启动”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-462">Select Start.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-463">在搜索框中键入 "设备管理器"，并在列表中选择它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-463">Type "device manager" in the search box and select it in the list.</span></span> 
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-464">展开 "Mixed reality 设备"，并查看是否列出了你的耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-464">Expand "Mixed reality devices" and see if your headset is listed.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="79562-465">如果未列出，请尝试以下操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-465">If it isn't listed, try the following:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-466">将耳机插入电脑上的不同端口（如果可用）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-466">Plug the headset into different ports on the PC, if available.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-467">查看 Windows 更新中的最新软件更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-467">Check for the latest software updates from Windows Update.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-468">卸载并重新安装 Windows Mixed Reality：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-468">Uninstall and reinstall Windows Mixed Reality:</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-469">从电脑拔下耳机电缆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-469">Disconnect both headset cables from your PC.</span></span>
    2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-470">选择 " **设置" > 混合现实 > 卸载** "。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-470">Select **Settings  > Mixed reality > Uninstall** .</span></span>
    3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-471">选择 " **设置" > 设备 > 蓝牙 & "其他设备** " 以取消配对运动控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-471">Select **Settings  > Devices  > Bluetooth & other devices** to unpair your motion controllers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-472">选择每个控制器，然后选择 "删除设备"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-472">Select each controller, and then select "Remove device".</span></span>
    4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-473">将您的耳机插回您的 PC 上，重新安装 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-473">Plug your headset back into your PC to reinstall Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span>
    
### <a name="im-getting-a-check-your-usb-cable-error-message"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-474">我收到 "检查 USB 电缆" 错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-474">I'm getting a "Check your USB cable" error message.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-475">将耳机连接到不同的 USB 端口 (，并确保它是 SuperSpeed USB 3.0) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-475">Connect your headset to a different USB port (and make sure it’s a SuperSpeed USB 3.0).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-476">同时，尝试删除耳机与计算机之间的所有扩展器或集线器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-476">Also, try removing any extenders or hubs between the headset and the computer.</span></span>

### <a name="im-getting-a-check-your-display-cable-error-message"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-477">我收到 "检查显示电缆" 错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-477">I'm getting a "Check your display cable" error message.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-478">请尝试以下做法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-478">Try the following:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-479">将耳机连接到 DisplayPort 1.2 或更高版本，1.4 或者连接到或更高版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-479">Connect your headset to a DisplayPort 1.2 or later, or HDMI 1.4 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-480">确保端口与电脑上最先进的图形卡相对应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-480">Make sure the port corresponds with the most advanced graphics card on your PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-481">如果使用的是适配器，请确保它支持4K。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-481">If you’re using an adapter, make sure it's 4K capable.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-482">尝试使用不同的 HDMI 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-482">Try using a different HDMI port.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-483">如果将外部监视器连接到 HDMI 端口，请尝试将其插入 DisplayPort，并将 HDMI 端口用于耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-483">If you have an external monitor plugged into an HDMI port, try plugging it into a DisplayPort instead, and use the HDMI port for your headset.</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="79562-513">7-5 / 2181038087-5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-513">7-5  / 2181038087-5</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="79562-514">**Windows Mixed Reality 连接到耳机时遇到问题。尝试将你的耳机插入其他 USB 端口，并暂时拔下连接到电脑的任何其他 USB 设备。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-514">**Windows Mixed Reality is having trouble connecting to your headset. Try plugging your headset into a different USB port and temporarily unplugging any other USB devices connected to your PC.**</span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="79562-515">Windows Mixed Reality 在混合现实摄像机帧时间戳和你的电脑时间戳之间丢失了同步。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-515">Windows Mixed Reality lost synchronization between the Mixed Reality camera frame timestamps and your PC timestamps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-516">这可能是暂时性错误，也可能是 USB 信号完整性问题的指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-516">This could be a transient error, or an indication of USB signal integrity issues.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-517">解决方法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-517">To fix this:</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="79562-518">暂时拔出所有 USB 设备和外围设备，取下所有延长电缆，并插入耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-518">Temporarily unplug all of your USB devices and peripherals, remove all extension cables, and plug in just your headset.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="79562-519">在电脑上禁用任何 USB 挂起/节能功能，如在 Windows 电源选项中选择性挂起、在 Windows 电源选项设备管理器中选择 "允许计算机关闭此设备以节省电源" 设置，以及 PC 固件中的任何 USB 节能设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-519">Disable any USB suspend/power saving features on your PC, like Selective suspend in Windows power options, the "Allow the computer to turn off this device to save power" setting in Device Manager, and any USB power saving settings in your PC's firmware.</span></span></li></ul>

|   <span data-ttu-id="79562-536">7-11 / 2181038087-11</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-536">7-11  / 2181038087-11</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="79562-537">**CPU 太旧，无法与 Windows Mixed Reality 兼容。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-537">**Your CPU is too old to be compatible with Windows Mixed Reality.**</span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="79562-538">你的电脑未通过兼容性检查，因为 CPU 缺少混合现实运动控制器所需的 AVX 指令集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-538">Your PC is failing the compatibility check because your CPU is missing the AVX instruction set required by the Mixed Reality motion controllers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-539">需要使用 [Windows Mixed Reality 兼容的 PC](https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/view-all-devices?col=wmr-pcs#icons)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-539">You'll need a [Windows Mixed Reality compatible PC](https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/view-all-devices?col=wmr-pcs#icons).</span></span>
|   <span data-ttu-id="79562-540">7-12 / 2181038087-12</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-540">7-12  / 2181038087-12</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="79562-541">**你的耳机连接到不兼容的 USB 控制器。尝试将你的耳机插入到其他 USB 端口（如果可用）。或者，尝试安装 Microsoft USB 驱动程序来代替任何不兼容的驱动程序。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-541">**Your headset is connected to an incompatible USB controller. Try plugging your headset into a different USB port, if available. Or, try installing a Microsoft USB driver in place of any incompatible drivers.**</span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="79562-542">你的耳机可能插入到连接到不兼容的非 Microsoft USB 控制器驱动程序的 USB 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-542">Your headset may be plugged in to a USB port connected to an incompatible non-Microsoft USB controller driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-543">这些 USB 3.0 控制器驱动程序通常不会读取和处理 [ContainerID 描述符](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows-hardware/drivers/usbcon/usb-containerids-in-windows)，这会将混合现实耳机的不同部分聚合到一个内聚的单元中 (以便从正确的耳机播放音频，视频输出正确的显示器，并从正确的传感器) 请求跟踪数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-543">These USB 3.0 controller drivers are often missing the ability to read and handle the [ContainerID descriptor](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows-hardware/drivers/usbcon/usb-containerids-in-windows), which aggregates the disparate parts of the Mixed Reality headset into a cohesive unit (to play audio out of the correct headphones, video out the correct displays, and pull tracking data from the correct sensors).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-544">更改 USB 控制器驱动程序：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-544">To change your USB controller driver:</span></span> <ol start="1"><li><span data-ttu-id="79562-545">启动设备管理器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-545">Launch Device Manager.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="79562-546">展开 "通用串行总线控制器" 的类别，然后单击右键，为包含 "可扩展主机控制器" 文本的每个项卸载驱动程序 **，** 名称中不包含 "Microsoft"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-546">Expand the category for Universal Serial Bus controllers and right click to uninstall the driver for each item that includes the text "eXtensible Host Controller" **and** does not have "Microsoft" in the name.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="79562-547">选择 "删除此设备的驱动程序软件" 以确保删除旧的驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-547">Select "Delete the driver software for this device" to ensure the old drivers are removed.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="79562-548">验证包含文本 "可扩展主机控制器" 的每个项在结尾都有 "Microsoft"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-548">Verify that each item that includes the text "eXtensible Host Controller" has "Microsoft" at the end.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="79562-549">插入 HMD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-549">Plug in the HMD.</span></span></li></ol><span data-ttu-id="79562-550">或者，如果此问题是间歇性的，则 HMD 可能无法正确响应 HMD 驱动程序中的命令。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-550">Alternatively, if the issue is intermittent, the HMD might not be properly responding to commands from the HMD driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-551">若要解决此问题，请将 HMD 拔出30或更多秒，并重新插入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-551">To fix, unplug the HMD for 30 or more seconds, then plug it back in.</span></span> | 
|   <span data-ttu-id="79562-552">7-13 / 2181038087-13</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-552">7-13  / 2181038087-13</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="79562-553">**你的耳机连接到不兼容的 USB 控制器。尝试将你的耳机插入到其他 USB 端口（如果可用）。如果没有，则需要安装新的 USB 3.0 控制器。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-553">**Your headset is connected to an incompatible USB controller. Try plugging your headset into a different USB port, if available. ## <a name="motion-controller-problems"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-622">运动控制器问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-622">Motion controller problems</span></span>

### <a name="my-motion-controllers-arent-working-properly"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-623">运动控制器不能正常工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-623">My Motion controllers aren't working properly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-624">如果 [运动控制器](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4040517/windows-10-controllers-windows-mixed-reality) 没有工作、未连接或在戴上耳机时看不到控制器的图像，请尝试以下操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-624">If your [motion controllers](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4040517/windows-10-controllers-windows-mixed-reality) aren’t working, aren't connecting, or if you don’t see an image of the controllers when you’re wearing your headset, try the following:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-625">请确保已打开控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-625">Make sure your controllers are turned on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-626">若要将其打开，请按住 Windows 按钮两秒钟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-626">To turn them on, press and hold the Windows button for two seconds.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-627">请确保控制器完全充电，如果不是，则更换电池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-627">Make sure the controllers are fully charged and replace the batteries if they are not.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-628">将控制器保持在您的前方，同时关闭控制器并将其打开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-628">Turn the controllers off and on again while holding them in front of you.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-629">按住 Windows 按钮四秒钟，使控制器关闭，然后再次按住该控制器两秒钟，以将其打开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-629">Press and hold the Windows button for four seconds to turn a controller off, then press and hold it again for two seconds to turn it on.</span></span> 
4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-630">选择 " **设置" > 设备 > 蓝牙 &** 计算机上的其他设备，并确保控制器已按配对方式列出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-630">Select **Settings > Devices > Bluetooth & other devices** on your PC and make sure the controllers are listed as paired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-631">如果不是，则需要将 [它们配对](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4040517/windows-10-controllers-windows-mixed-reality)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-631">If they’re not, you’ll need to [pair them](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4040517/windows-10-controllers-windows-mixed-reality).</span></span> 
5. <span data-ttu-id="79562-632">请确保运动控制器显示为 "已连接"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-632">Make sure the motion controllers show up as "Connected".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-633">"配对" 不一定表示控制器已连接到 PC。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-633">"Paired" does not necessarily mean the controllers are connected to the PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-634">控制器应出现在 "鼠标，键盘 & 笔" 类别下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-634">Controllers should appear under "Mouse, keyboard & pen" category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-635">"其他设备" 下的运动控制器未通过配对过程，因此不起作用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-635">Motion controllers under "Other devices" have failed the pairing process and are not functional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-636">检查运动控制器 Led 指示灯：强光亮起的控制器已配对并且已连接，dimly 发亮控制器未连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-636">Check the motion controllers LEDs: Brightly lit controllers are paired and connected, dimly lit controllers aren't connected.</span></span>
6. <span data-ttu-id="79562-637">在电脑上，请参阅 **开始 > 混合现实门户** ，并选择 "菜单"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-637">Go to **Start  > Mixed Reality Portal** on your PC and select "Menu".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-638">你应该会看到你的运动控制器以及状态消息：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-638">You should see your motion controllers listed, along with a status message:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-639">就绪–控制器都已设置好。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-639">Ready – The controllers are all set.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-640">丢失跟踪–混合现实门户找不到控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-640">Lost tracking – Mixed Reality Portal can’t find your controllers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-641">将其放在头戴戴显示设备前面，按 "Windows" 按钮4秒钟再重新启动，然后再次2秒钟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-641">Hold them in front of your headset and restart them by pressing the Windows button for 4 seconds, then again for 2 seconds.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="79562-642">电池电量低–更换控制器电池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-642">Low battery – Replace the controller batteries.</span></span>
7. <span data-ttu-id="79562-643">如果使用的是外部 USB 蓝牙适配器，请确保将其插入到黑色 USB 2.0 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-643">If you're using an external USB Bluetooth Adapter, make sure it’s plugged into a black USB 2.0 port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-644">还应尽可能远离任何其他无线发送器或 USB 闪存驱动器（包括耳机的 USB 连接器）连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-644">It should also be plugged in as far away as possible from any other wireless transmitters or USB flash drives, including the USB connector for your headset.</span></span> 
8. <span data-ttu-id="79562-645">通过右键单击 Windows "开始" 菜单并选择 "设备管理器"，验证 PC 中是否只有一个蓝牙收音机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-645">Verify that there’s only one Bluetooth radio in the PC by right clicking on the Windows Start Menu and select Device Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-646">展开 "蓝牙" 部分，并查找一个适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-646">Expand the Bluetooth section and look for one Adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-647">如果你使用的是带内置收音机的台式计算机配置，请检查是否已连接外部天线。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-647">If you are using the desktop PC configuration with built-in radio, check if an external antenna is connected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-648">如果未连接外部天线，则可能会导致跟踪问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-648">If there is no external antenna connected, it can cause tracking issues.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-649">或使用外部蓝牙转换器 (USB) ，禁用内部蓝牙功能，然后重试配对和连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-649">Or use an external bluetooth dongle (USB), disable the internal Bluetooth capability, and retry pairing and connecting.</span></span>
9. <span data-ttu-id="79562-650">关闭蓝牙设置窗口（如果已打开）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-650">Close the Bluetooth settings window if it's open.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-651">如果在后台打开，则需要对蓝牙协议进行大量的额外调用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-651">If it is open in the background, a lot of extra calls are made to the Bluetooth protocol.</span></span>
10. <span data-ttu-id="79562-652">检查运动控制器上的虚拟电池电量水平。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-652">Check the virtual battery level on the motion controller.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-653">在混合现实中，打开控制器，可以看到电池图标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-653">In mixed reality, turn the controllers over, and you'll be able to see a battery icon.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-654">如果它是红色，请更换电池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-654">If it is red, replace the batteries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-655">通常，在连接控制器后，电池报告会报告高于实际水平。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-655">Battery reporting typically reports higher than the actual level immediately after connecting a controller.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-656">等待大约15秒钟，让电池电量稳定，然后阅读该级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-656">Wait about 15 seconds to let the battery level stabilize and then read the level.</span></span>
11. <span data-ttu-id="79562-657">**> 设备 > 蓝牙 & 其他设备** 中删除蓝牙耳机和扬声器，并关闭设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-657">Remove Bluetooth headphones and speakers in **Settings > Devices > Bluetooth & other devices** , and turn the devices off.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-658">在混合现实耳机上使用耳机插孔或内置扬声器获得最佳音频体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-658">Use the headphone jack or built-in speakers on your Mixed Reality headset for the best audio experience.</span></span>
12. <span data-ttu-id="79562-659">如果你有与电脑配对的其他蓝牙设备，如耳机或 gamepads，请将其删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-659">If you have other Bluetooth devices paired with your PC, such as headphones or gamepads, remove some of them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-660">选择 " **设置" > 设备上 > 蓝牙 & 其他设备** "，选择设备，然后选择" 删除设备 "。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-660">Select **Settings > Devices > Bluetooth & other devices on your PC** , select the devices, and then select "Remove device".</span></span>
13. <span data-ttu-id="79562-661">拔出耳机上的 USB 电缆，并将其重新插回计算机，以便在电脑上重新启动控制器功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-661">Unplug the USB cable on your headset and plugging it back into the PC to restart the controller functionality on the PC.</span></span>
14. <span data-ttu-id="79562-662">当控制器正在进行固件更新时，它会闪烁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-662">Controller lights flash when they are undergoing a firmware update.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-663">等待固件更新完成，控制器应显示为混合现实。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-663">Wait for the firmware update to complete and the controllers should appear in Mixed Reality.</span></span>
15. <span data-ttu-id="79562-664">确保你的电脑已连接到 5GHz Wi-fi 网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-664">Make sure your PC is connected to a 5GHz Wi-Fi network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-665">如果便携式计算机连接到 2.4 GHz Wifi 网络，则通常会共享蓝牙连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-665">If your laptop is connected to a 2.4GHz Wifi network, it is typically sharing the Bluetooth connection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-666">这可能会对 Wifi 或蓝牙性能产生负面影响，具体取决于产品设计。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-666">This may negatively impact either Wifi or Bluetooth performance, depending on the product design.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-667">在网络适配器设置中将首选带区更改为5Ghz。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-667">Change the preferred band to 5Ghz in the network adapter settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-668">如果网络不支持5GHz，则可以使用蓝牙转换器，而不是使用内部蓝牙功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-668">If your network does not support 5GHz, a Bluetooth dongle can be used instead of the internal Bluetooth capability.</span></span>
16. <span data-ttu-id="79562-669">如果你的蓝牙设置已经配对了运动控制器，则在删除这些设备之前，Windows 将不会发现这些新设备 (如果已使用特定的转换器添加这些设备，则只能使用该转换器) 来删除它们。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-669">If your Bluetooth settings have motion controllers already paired, Windows won’t discover the new devices until those are removed (if they have been added using a specific dongle, they can be only removed with that dongle).</span></span>
17. <span data-ttu-id="79562-670">如果你的电脑具有内置的蓝牙，并且你有连接问题，请尝试改用 USB 蓝牙适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-670">If your PC has built-in Bluetooth and you’re having connection problems, try using a USB Bluetooth adapter instead.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-671">为此，需要在设备管理器关闭内置蓝牙无线电，然后将其他蓝牙设备与新的适配器配对。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-671">To do this, you’ll need to turn off your built-in Bluetooth radio in Device Manager and then pair your other Bluetooth devices with the new adapter.</span></span>

### <a name="motion-controller-troubleshooting-flowchart"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-672">运动控制器疑难解答流程图</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-672">Motion controller troubleshooting flowchart</span></span>

### <a name="my-controller-is-stuck-in-an-infinite-reboot-buzzing-after-leds-cycle"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-674">) Led 循环后，控制器停滞在无限重启 (。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-674">My controller is stuck in an infinite reboot (buzzing after LEDs cycle).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-675">这是一个关键电池指示器，因此请确保设备中有新电池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-675">This is a critical battery indicator, so make sure you have fresh batteries in the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-676">如果问题仍然存在，请执行 [设备恢复](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-restore-the-controllers-to-factory-settings) ，将控制器重置为出厂设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-676">If the issue persists, perform [device recovery](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-restore-the-controllers-to-factory-settings) to reset the controller to factory settings.</span></span>

### <a name="im-trying-to-pair-my-controllers-but-they-never-show-up-in-the-add-a-new-device-menu-in-bluetooth-settings"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-677">我尝试配对控制器，但它们永远不会显示在蓝牙设置的 "添加新的设备菜单" 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-677">I'm trying to pair my controllers, but they never show up in the "Add a new device menu" in Bluetooth Settings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-678">请检查是否已将控制器配对，请将其删除，然后重试。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-678">Check that you do not have controllers paired already, remove them and try again.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-679">如果问题仍然存在，请重新启动计算机，然后重试。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-679">If problem persists restart the PC and try again.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-680">如果失败，请参阅 [蓝牙常见问题解答](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-tell-if-im-using-bluetooth-technology)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-680">If that fails, consult the [Bluetooth FAQs](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-tell-if-im-using-bluetooth-technology).</span></span>

### <a name="wi-fi-speeds-becomes-slow-on-my-notebook-when-motion-controllers-are-turned-on"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-681">当动作控制器开启时，笔记本的 wi-fi 速度会变慢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-681">Wi-Fi speeds becomes slow on my notebook when motion controllers are turned on.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-682">当连接到 2.4 GHz 接入点时，笔记本可能与蓝牙共享其 Wi-fi 天线。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-682">Your notebook may share its Wi-Fi antenna with Bluetooth when connected to 2.4GHz access point.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-683">如果可以将带区首选项切换到5GHz，请从设备管理器中进行检查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-683">Check from device manager if you can switch band preference to 5GHz.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-684">如果5GHz 网络不可用并且性能受到严重影响，请考虑使用蓝牙转换器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-684">If 5GHz network is not available and performance is severely impacted, consider using a Bluetooth dongle.</span></span>

![可以通过设备管理器找到 Wifi 波段选择设置](images/wifi5ghz.png)

### <a name="my-second-controller-takes-a-long-time-to-reconnect"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-686">第二个控制器需要很长时间才能重新连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-686">My second controller takes a long time to reconnect.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-687">如果同时打开了运动控制器，某些较早的 Intel 无线电系统会出现此问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-687">Some older Intel radios experience this issue if motion controllers are powered on at the same time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-688">避免同时打开控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-688">Avoid powering on controllers at the same time.</span></span>

### <a name="my-qualcomm-bluetooth-radio-cannot-pair-controllers-after-a-pc-crash"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-689">在电脑崩溃后，Qualcomm 蓝牙无线电无法配对控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-689">My Qualcomm Bluetooth radio cannot pair controllers after a PC crash.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-690">Qualcomm (QCA) 在 Windows 崩溃后，10.0.0.448 之前的蓝牙无线电驱动程序可能会以错误状态结束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-690">Qualcomm (QCA) Bluetooth radio drivers prior to 10.0.0.448 may end up in bad state after a Windows crash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-691">完全关闭 PC 以解决此问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-691">Power off the PC completely to workaround this problem.</span></span> 

### <a name="im-experiencing-poor-controller-tracking-with-marvell-radio"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-692">我通过 Marvell 收音机遇到控制器跟踪问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-692">I'm experiencing poor controller tracking with Marvell radio.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-693">请参阅 **设备管理器 > 蓝牙 > MARVELL AVASTAR 蓝牙无线电适配器 > 属性 > 驱动程序** ，并确保使用的是 driver 15.68.9210.47 或更高版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-693">Go to **Device Manager > Bluetooth > Marvell AVASTAR Bluetooth Radio Adapter > Properties > Driver** and make sure that you are using driver 15.68.9210.47 or later.</span></span>

### <a name="the-mixed-reality-portal-is-working-but-my-motion-controllers-are-tracking-poorly-controllers-keep-flying-away-shaking-etc"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-694">混合现实门户正在运行，但运动控制器跟踪性能不佳 (控制器保持飞行、摇动等 ) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-694">The Mixed Reality Portal is working, but my motion controllers are tracking poorly (controllers keep flying away, shaking, etc.).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-695">某些照明条件可能会影响跟踪。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-695">Some lighting conditions can affect tracking.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-696">请确保未向直射直射，并确保您的 HMD (看不到很多的点光源，例如，如圣诞节树) 的灯光字符串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-696">Make sure that you are not exposed to direct sunlight and that you don't have a lot of point light sources visible to your HMD (for example, strings of lights like a christmas tree).</span></span> 
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-697">查看 [蓝牙常见问题解答](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-tell-if-im-using-bluetooth-technology)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-697">Check the [Bluetooth FAQs](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-tell-if-im-using-bluetooth-technology).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-698">这些症状通常是由于控制器与主机之间的通信失败引起的，并指示蓝牙链接质量较差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-698">These symptoms are generally caused by failures to communicate between the controller and the host PC, and indicate poor Bluetooth link quality.</span></span>

### <a name="motion-controller-leds-are-not-lit-but-the-buttons-and-thumbstick-still-work-in-mixed-reality-portal"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-699">运动控制器 Led 未亮起，但按钮和操纵杆仍适用于混合现实门户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-699">Motion Controller LEDs are not lit, but the buttons and thumbstick still work in Mixed Reality Portal.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-700">运动控制器校准缓存可能已损坏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-700">The Motion Controller calibration cache may be corrupt.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-701">若要删除缓存，请在管理员命令提示符下运行以下命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-701">To delete the cache, run the following command in an Administrator Command Prompt:</span></span>

`rmdir /S /Q C:\Windows\ServiceProfiles\LocalService\AppData\Local\Microsoft\Windows\MotionController\Calibration`

<span data-ttu-id="79562-702">此文件夹在 Windows 资源管理器中不可访问，只能从管理员命令提示符中修改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-702">This folder is not accessible in Windows Explorer and can only be modified from an Administrator Command Prompt.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-703">删除文件夹后，请重新启动计算机，然后重新连接运动控制器以还原校准文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-703">After you have deleted the folder, restart your PC and reconnect your Motion Controllers to restore the calibration files.</span></span>

### <a name="motion-controllers-do-not-appear-in-steamvr-apps-and-games"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-704">运动控制器不会出现在 SteamVR 的应用和游戏中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-704">Motion controllers do not appear in SteamVR apps and games.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-705">如果可以在 cliff 房子中看到运动控制器，而不是在 SteamVR 应用和游戏中查看，则可能是运动控制器型号驱动程序安装不正确。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-705">If you're able to see your Motion Controllers in the cliff house, but not in SteamVR apps and games, the Motion Controller model driver may not be installed properly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-706">此驱动程序通过 Windows 更新自动下载和安装，但如果你在具有企业策略的 PC 上，或者如果 Windows 更新受到限制，则可能需要手动安装此驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-706">This driver is automatically downloaded and installed via Windows Update, but if you're on a PC that has enterprise policies or if Windows Update is otherwise restricted, you may need to install this manually.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-707">检查运动控制器型号驱动程序是否正确安装：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-707">To check that the Motion Controller model driver is correctly installed:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-708">打开这两个运动控制器，并确保它们在 "设备" 下的 "设置" 应用中显示为 "已连接" **> Bluetooth & 其他设备** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-708">Turn on both of your motion controllers, and make sure they show up as "Connected" in the Settings app under **Devices > Bluetooth & other devices** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-709">如果它们没有显示，或者显示为 "配对"，请将 [它们配对](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/set-up-windows-mixed-reality)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-709">If they do not show up or show up as "Paired", [pair them](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/set-up-windows-mixed-reality).</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-710">打开设备管理器并在 "蓝牙" 下查找 "运动控制器-左" 和 "运动控制器-右"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-710">Open Device Manager and look for "Motion controller - Left" and "Motion controller - Right" under "Bluetooth".</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-711">选择任一设备，然后 **按连接查看 > 设备** "。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-711">Select either device and then go to **View > Devices by Connection** .</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-712">现在，你将看到动作控制器蓝牙设备的视图汇总到蓝牙收音机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-712">You will now see a view of the Motion Controller Bluetooth devices roll up to your Bluetooth radio.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-713">在与两个运动控制器相同的节点下，应该有两个 "蓝牙 HID 设备" 设备，并且在每个蓝牙 HID 设备下，都应该是名为 "运动控制器" 的设备，并) 灰色图标 (。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-713">Under the same node as the two Motion Controllers should be two "Bluetooth HID Device" devices, and under each Bluetooth HID Device should be devices named "Motion Controller" (with gray icons).</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="79562-714">双击每个 "运动控制器" 设备，然后单击 " **驱动程序** " 选项卡。确认列出的驱动程序版本与 [其中一个运动控制器型号驱动程序版本](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/mixed-reality-software#mixed-reality-motion-controller-model-driver-release-history)相对应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-714">Double click each of the "Motion Controller" devices and go to the **Driver** tab. Confirm that the Driver Version listed corresponds to one of [these Motion Controller model driver versions](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/mixed-reality-software#mixed-reality-motion-controller-model-driver-release-history).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-715">若要手动下载和安装运动控制器模型驱动程序，请访问 [此页](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/mixed-reality-software#mixed-reality-motion-controller-model-driver-release-history) ，并查找与你的 Windows 10 版本对应的驱动程序版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-715">To manually download and install the Motion Controller model driver, visit [this page](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/mixed-reality-software#mixed-reality-motion-controller-model-driver-release-history) and look for the driver version corresponding to your version of Windows 10.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-716">下载页上提供了安装说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-716">Installation instructions are available on the download page.</span></span>

### <a name="the-motion-controllers-firmware-update-takes-significantly-longer-than-two-minutes"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-717">运动控制器固件更新所需的时间明显超过两分钟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-717">The Motion controllers firmware update takes significantly longer than two minutes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-718">查看 [蓝牙常见问题解答](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-tell-if-im-using-bluetooth-technology)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-718">Check the [Bluetooth FAQs](motion-controller-problems.md#how-can-i-tell-if-im-using-bluetooth-technology).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-719">通常不太常见的蓝牙链接质量导致了这些问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-719">Poor Bluetooth link quality is usually the cause of these problems.</span></span>

### <a name="i-just-inserted-fresh-batteries-but-the-controller-virtual-battery-level-does-not-indicate-full-level"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-720">我刚插入了新电池，但控制器虚拟电池电量不表示完全水平。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-720">I just inserted fresh batteries but the controller virtual battery level does not indicate full level.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-721">为 AA 电池调整了运动控制器电池电量水平。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-721">Motion controller battery level is tuned for AA batteries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-722">即使完全充电，某些低电压充电电池也可能不会报告为完整。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-722">Some low voltage rechargeable batteries may not report as full although being fully charged.</span></span>

### <a name="my-controller-does-not-vibrate-when-battery-is-low"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-723">当电池电量低时，控制器不振动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-723">My controller does not vibrate when battery is low.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-724">电池电量降低时，将禁用 Haptics。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-724">Haptics is disabled when battery level gets low.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-725">更换电池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-725">Replace your batteries.</span></span>

### <a name="my-device-vibrated-three-times-and-then-shutdown"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-726">我的设备 vibrated 三次，然后关闭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-726">My device vibrated three times and then shutdown.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-727">电池电量不足，并达到切削阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-727">Your batteries are running low and hit the cut-off threshold.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-728">更换电池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-728">Replace your batteries.</span></span>

### <a name="my-samsung-motion-controllers-touchpad-is-off-center-or-has-a-dead-spot"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-729">我的 Samsung 运动控制器的触摸板处于离线状态或具有死点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-729">My Samsung motion controller’s touchpad is off-center or has a dead spot.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-730">这可能是硬件缺陷，应返回给零售商或设备制造商提供更换或交换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-730">This is probably a hardware defect and you should go back to your retailer or equipment manufacturer for a replacement or exchange.</span></span>

### <a name="the-controller-isnt-working-correctly-and-i-cant-update-the-device"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-731">控制器工作不正常，无法更新设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-731">The controller isn't working correctly and I can't update the device.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-732">将其还原为出厂条件 (需要全新电池) ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-732">Restore it to factory conditions (you will need fresh batteries):</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-733">拔出并关闭控制器电源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-733">Unplug and power off the controllers.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-734">打开电池盖子。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-734">Open the battery cover.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-735">插入新电池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-735">Insert your new batteries.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-736">按住 "配对" 按钮 (电池) 下底部的选项卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-736">Press and hold the pairing button (the tab at the bottom under the batteries).</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="79562-737">按住 "配对" 按钮时，通过按住 Windows 按钮5秒钟来打开控制器， (使这两个按钮按下) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-737">While holding the pairing button, power on the controller by pressing and holding the Windows button for five seconds (keep both buttons depressed).</span></span>
6. <span data-ttu-id="79562-738">释放按钮并等待控制器开启。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-738">Release the buttons and wait for controller to power on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-739">这最多需要15秒的时间，并且在发生设备恢复时不会出现任何迹象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-739">This takes up to 15 seconds and there are no indicators when device recovery is happening.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-740">如果设备在立即开机，则表明 "恢复" 按钮序列未注册，需要重试。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-740">If device powers on immediately on button release, the recovery button sequence did not get registered and you need to try again.</span></span>
7. <span data-ttu-id="79562-741">中转到 " **设置" > bluetooth > 其他设备** "，然后选择" 运动控制器-左 "或" 运动控制器-右 "和" 删除设备 ") ，从蓝牙设置中删除旧的控制器关联。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-741">Go to **Settings > Bluetooth > other devices** , and select "Motion controller - Left" or "Motion controller - Right" and "Remove device") to remove old controller associations from Bluetooth settings.</span></span> 
8. <span data-ttu-id="79562-742">再次将控制器与电脑配对。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-742">Pair the controller with the PC again.</span></span>
9. <span data-ttu-id="79562-743">连接到主机和 HMD 后，设备将更新到最新的可用固件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-743">After connecting with the host and HMD, the device will update to the latest available firmware.</span></span>

### <a name="lights-and-indicators"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-744">光源和指示器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-744">Lights and indicators</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-745">LED 星座环形和 haptics 指示运动控制器的状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-745">The LED constellation ring and haptics indicate the state of the motion controller.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="79562-746">状态</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-746">State</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="79562-747">导致状态的原因</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-747">What causes the state</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="79562-748">与状态关联的光线和振动行为</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-748">Light and vibration behavior associated with the state</span></span> |
|----------------------------|-----------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="79562-749">**开机**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-749">**Power on**</span></span>               | <span data-ttu-id="79562-750">按住控制器上的 Windows 按钮两秒钟，以打开控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-750">Press and hold Windows button on controller for two seconds to turn on the controller.</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="79562-751">Led 打开，控制器 vibrates 一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-751">LEDs turn on and controller vibrates once.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="79562-752">**关机**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-752">**Power off**</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="79562-753">按住控制器上的 Windows 按钮四秒钟以关闭控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-753">Press and hold Windows button on controller for four seconds to turn off controller.</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="79562-754">Led 关闭，控制器 vibrates 两次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-754">LEDs turn off and controller vibrates twice.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="79562-755">**Sleeping**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-755">**Sleeping**</span></span>               | <span data-ttu-id="79562-756">当控制器 motionless 30 秒时，控制器会自动进入睡眠状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-756">The controller enters sleeping state automatically when it’s motionless for 30 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-757">控制器在检测到运动时将自动唤醒，但设备未与主机 PC 配对的情况除外。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-757">The controller automatically wakes when it detects motion except when the device is not paired with the host PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-758">在这种情况下，需要按按钮才能唤醒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-758">In that case, a button press will be required to wake it up.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="79562-759">处于睡眠状态时，指示灯关闭并每隔三秒闪烁一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-759">LEDs turn off and blink every three seconds while in sleeping state.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="79562-760">**组合**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-760">**Pairing**</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="79562-761">在电池大小写内按住配对按钮三秒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-761">Press and hold pairing button inside battery case for three seconds.</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="79562-762">Led 在配对模式下缓慢脉冲，并在退出配对模式时转为稳定状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-762">LEDs slowly pulse while in pairing mode, and go solid when exiting pairing mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-763">如果配对成功，则控制器 vibrates 一次; 如果配对失败并超时，则为 vibrates 三次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-763">The controller vibrates once if pairing was successful or vibrates three times if pairing is unsuccessful and times out.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="79562-764">**控制器连接/断开与电脑的连接**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-764">**Controller connects/disconnects from PC**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="79562-765">控制器成功连接后，控制器已成功连接到 PC，或在使用时控制器断开连接，因为某种原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-765">The controller successfully connects to PC after you turn it on, or the controller disconnects from the PC during use for some reason.</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="79562-766">控制器 vibrates 计算机连接或断开连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-766">The controller vibrates once on PC connection or disconnection.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="79562-767">**低电池电量水平**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-767">**Low Battery Level**</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="79562-768">电池电量低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-768">The battery level is low.</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="79562-769">电池电量不足时没有 LED 或振动指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-769">There is no LED or vibration indication when battery is low.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-770">耳机上控制器表示形式的句柄上有一个电池指示器图标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-770">There is a battery indicator icon on the handle of the controller representation in headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-771">当电池电量低时，指示器图标将显示1/4。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-771">When battery is low, the indicator icon will show 1/4 full.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="79562-772">**严重电池电量水平**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-772">**Critical Battery Level**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="79562-773">当电池电量为 "关键" 时开机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-773">During power on when battery level is "Critical".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-774">"严重" 电池电量表示电量不足，控制器将自动关闭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-774">"Critical" battery level means there is insufficient power and the controller will turn off automatically.</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="79562-775">控制器 vibrates 三次，并在打开时自动关闭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-775">The controller vibrates three times when you turn it on and then automatically turns off.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-776">当你使用此状态时，电池指示器图标将显示红色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-776">As you approach this state, the battery indicator icon will display red.</span></span> |


### <a name="how-can-i-tell-if-im-using-bluetooth-technology"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-777">如何判断我是否在使用蓝牙技术？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-777">How can I tell if I'm using Bluetooth technology?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-778">运动控制器使用在许多消费者设备中找到的相同蓝牙技术，其设计目的是使用任何最近的 PC 中包含的蓝牙功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-778">Motion controllers use the same Bluetooth technology found in many consumer devices and are designed to work with the Bluetooth capability included in any recent PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-779">若要验证你的计算机是否具有蓝牙无线电 (设备是否已通过混合现实兼容性检查器) ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-779">To verify that your PC has a Bluetooth radio (it should if the device passed the Mixed Reality Compatibility Checker):</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-780">右键单击 Windows "开始" 菜单，然后选择 "设备管理器"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-780">Right click on the Windows Start Menu and select "Device Manager".</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-781">展开 "蓝牙" 部分，并查找适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-781">Expand the Bluetooth section and look for an adapter.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-782">如果你的电脑没有蓝牙，则建议使用一个 [PLUGABLE USB 蓝牙4.0 低能量微适配器](https://www.amazon.com/Plugable-Bluetooth-Adapter-Raspberry-Compatible/dp/B009ZIILLI/ref=sr-1-1?ie=UTF8&qid=1490148230&sr=8-1&keywords=plugable+broadcom)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-782">If your PC doesn’t have Bluetooth, one recommended dongle is the [Plugable USB Bluetooth 4.0 Low Energy Micro Adapter](https://www.amazon.com/Plugable-Bluetooth-Adapter-Raspberry-Compatible/dp/B009ZIILLI/ref=sr-1-1?ie=UTF8&qid=1490148230&sr=8-1&keywords=plugable+broadcom).\</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="79562-783">![示例设备管理器的屏幕截图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-783">![Screenshot of an Example Device Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-784">适配器是蓝牙收音机。](images/devicemanagerbtadapterpic.png)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-784">The Adapter is the Bluetooth radio.](images/devicemanagerbtadapterpic.png)</span></span> 


### <a name="my-pc-has-bluetooth-technology-but-im-having-problems-with-my-motion-controllers"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-785">我的 PC 具有蓝牙技术，但我的运动控制器有问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-785">My PC has Bluetooth technology but I'm having problems with my motion controllers.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-786">动作控制器应与其他蓝牙键盘、鼠标和游戏控制器一起工作，但体验会因使用的键盘、鼠标或游戏控制器的型号而异。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-786">Motion controllers should work with other Bluetooth keyboards, mice, and game controllers, but the experience will vary depending on the model of keyboard, mouse, or game controller you use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-787">可以执行以下操作来提高性能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-787">Here are some things you can do to improve performance:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-788">如果你的计算机具有蓝牙功能，但运动控制器仍有问题，请考虑将蓝牙无线电替换为插入到 USB 的 Plugable 外部蓝牙适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-788">If your computer has Bluetooth but you are still having problems with the motion controllers, consider replacing your Bluetooth radio with the Plugable external Bluetooth Adapter plugged into USB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-789">请注意，一次只能有一个蓝牙无线电适配器处于活动状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-789">Note that you can only have one Bluetooth radio adapter active at a time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-790">如果除了插入现有收音机外，还插入外部广播，则需要在设备管理器中禁用现有蓝牙无线电 (右键单击该适配器，然后选择 "禁用设备" ) 并取消对以前的所有蓝牙设备的配对。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-790">If you plug in an external radio in addition to an existing radio you need to disable your existing Bluetooth radio in Device Manager (right click on the adapter and select "Disable Device") and un-pair/re-pair all of your previous Bluetooth devices.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-791">如果使用的是 USB 蓝牙适配器，请将其连接到 USB 2.0 端口 (2.0 端口为黑色，未标记为 "SS" ) （如果可用）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-791">If you're using a USB Bluetooth Adapter, connect it to a USB 2.0 port (2.0 ports are black and aren’t labeled "SS"), if available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-792">端口应以物理方式与以下内容分开：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-792">The port should be physically separated from:</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="79562-793">HMD USB 连接器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-793">the HMD USB connector</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="79562-794">闪存驱动器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-794">flash drives</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="79562-795">硬盘驱动器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-795">hard drives</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="79562-796">无线 USB 接收器（如键盘/鼠标键盘的理想接收方）理想情况下，从这些其他连接器将 USB 蓝牙适配器插入到计算机的另一侧。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-796">wireless USB receivers like those for keyboards/mice Ideally, plug the USB Bluetooth Adapter into the opposite side of the computer as far as possible from these other connectors.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-797">不要安装任何第三方软件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-797">Do not install any third party software.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-798">关闭蓝牙设置窗口（如果已打开）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-798">Close the Bluetooth settings window if it's open.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-799">使其在后台处于打开状态，这意味着需要对蓝牙协议进行大量的额外调用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-799">Leaving it open in the background means that a lot of extra calls are made to the Bluetooth protocol.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-800">禁用蓝牙 & "其他设备" 下的 "显示通知以便使用 Swift 对进行连接" 设置，以减少主机收音机扫描活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-800">Disable "Show notification to connect using Swift Pair" setting under Bluetooth & other devices to reduce host radio scanning activity.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-801">如果使用的是内部蓝牙卡，请确保使用的是外部蓝牙天线。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-801">If you are using an internal Bluetooth card, please ensure you are using an external Bluetooth antenna.</span></span> 
  * <span data-ttu-id="79562-802">在这种情况下缺少外部蓝牙天线会导致跟踪问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-802">Lack of external Bluetooth antenna in this case is known to cause tracking issues.</span></span> 
  * <span data-ttu-id="79562-803">如果此操作不起作用，请在禁用内部蓝牙后 (USB) 使用外部蓝牙转换器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-803">If this doesn’t work, please use an external Bluetooth dongle (USB) after disabling the internal Bluetooth.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-804">设备在蓝牙设置中的 "鼠标、键盘 & 笔" 类别下出现，这一点很重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-804">It is important that the device appears under the "Mouse, Keyboard & Pen" category in the Bluetooth settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-805">如果在 "其他设备" 下，则取消配对并配对设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-805">If under "Other devices" then unpair and pair the device.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-806">删除、取消配对蓝牙耳机和扬声器电源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-806">Remove, un-pair, and power off Bluetooth headphones and speakers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-807">Windows Mixed Reality 不支持这些。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-807">These are not supported with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-808">可以在混合现实耳机上使用耳机插孔或内置扬声器获得最佳音频体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-808">You can use the headphone jack or built-in speakers on your Mixed Reality headset for the best audio experience.</span></span>

### <a name="how-can-i-pair-my-motion-controllers-to-a-windows-mixed-reality-headset-with-built-in-bluetooth-radio-or-return-them-to-their-factory-pairing"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-809">如何将我的运动控制器与内置蓝牙收音机的 Windows Mixed Reality 耳机配对，或将其返回给工厂配对？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-809">How can I pair my motion controllers to a Windows Mixed Reality headset with built-in Bluetooth radio, or return them to their factory pairing?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-810">某些 Windows Mixed Reality 耳机，包括 Acer OJO 500 和 Samsung 太空 +，内置蓝牙无线电收发器用于运动控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-810">Some Windows Mixed Reality headsets, including the Acer OJO 500 and Samsung Odyssey+, have built-in Bluetooth radios for use with motion controllers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-811">这些耳机附带的运动控制器与工厂中的耳机预配对，无需您的 PC 具有单独的蓝牙收音机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-811">The motion controllers that come with these headsets are pre-paired to the headset from the factory, and do not require your PC to have a separate Bluetooth radio.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-812">例如， _可以_ 将这些运动控制器手动配对到您的 PC 的蓝牙无线电设备，以与没有内置蓝牙无线电收发器的 Windows Mixed Reality 耳机配合使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-812">These motion controllers _can_ be manually paired to your PC's Bluetooth radio, for example, for use with Windows Mixed Reality headsets that do not have built-in Bluetooth radios.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-813">若要将运动控制器返回到工厂配对，或将其与带有内置蓝牙收音机的 Windows Mixed Reality 耳机配对，请运行耳机的设备附带应用 (例如，"Acer OJO 500" 应用或 "Samsung HMD 太空 + 安装" 应用程序，在首次将耳机插入) 时自动安装，并按照运动控制器配对的说明进行操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-813">To return the motion controllers to their factory pairing, or to pair them with a Windows Mixed Reality headset with built-in Bluetooth radio, run the headset's device companion app (for example, the "Acer OJO 500" app or the "Samsung HMD Odyssey+ Setup" app, automatically installed the first time the headset is plugged in) and follow the instructions for motion controller pairing.</span></span>


## <a name="performance-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-814">性能问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-814">Performance questions</span></span>

### <a name="how-can-i-tell-if-the-windows-mixed-reality-headset-is-rendering-at-60hz-or-90hz-framerate"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-815">如何判断 Windows Mixed Reality 耳机是否以60Hz 或90Hz 的帧速率呈现？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-815">How can I tell if the Windows Mixed Reality headset is rendering at 60Hz or 90Hz framerate?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-816">检查 **设备门户 > 性能** "选项卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-816">Check the **Device Portal > Performance** tab.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="79562-817">**注意** ：如果有与 HDMI 2.0 端口的离散 GPU 和具有4个或更多物理内核的 CPU，则应该获得 90 Hz。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-817">**Note** : If you have a discrete GPU with HDMI 2.0 ports and a CPU with four or more physical cores, you should be getting 90 Hz.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-818">如果 GPU 仅有 HDMI 1.4 输出，可以使用 DisplayPort 到 [HDMI 2.0 适配器](https://holodocswiki.com/wiki/Recommended_adapters_for_Windows_Mixed_Reality_Capable_PCs) 作为解决方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-818">If your GPU only has a HDMI 1.4 output, you can use a DisplayPort to [HDMI 2.0 adapter](https://holodocswiki.com/wiki/Recommended_adapters_for_Windows_Mixed_Reality_Capable_PCs) as a workaround.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="79562-819">**注意** ： **耳机显示 > 视觉质量设置** 仅影响 Windows Mixed Reality 主体验的呈现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-819">**Note** : The **Headset display > visual quality settings** only affect the rendering of the Windows Mixed Reality Home experience.</span></span>

### <a name="what-do-i-do-if-my-pc-appears-to-be-running-slowly"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-820">如果我的 PC 看起来运行缓慢，我该怎么办？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-820">What do I do if my PC appears to be running slowly?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-821">由于许多原因，系统可能会缓慢，在大多数情况下，这会在几秒钟后下降。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-821">The system may be sluggish for many reasons and in most cases this will subside after a few seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-822">如果在很长一段时间内遇到此问题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-822">If you experience this problem over long periods of time:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-823">关闭桌面上所有未使用的应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-823">Close all unused application on the desktop.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-824">确保便携式计算机已插入电源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-824">Ensure that your laptop is plugged into a power source.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-825">确保电脑未预热。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-825">Ensure that the PC is not warming up.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-826">降低 Windows Mixed Reality 主页的视觉质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-826">Lower the visual quality in your Windows Mixed Reality Home.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="79562-827">请确保具有最新的 PC 图形驱动程序 (参阅图形驱动程序部分) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-827">Ensure that you have the latest graphics drivers for your PC (see the graphics drivers section).</span></span>

### <a name="my-pc-is-warming-up-as-i-run-the-mixed-reality-experiences-how-do-i-keep-it-cool"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-828">我的 PC 正在预热，因为我运行了混合现实体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-828">My PC is warming up as I run the Mixed Reality experiences.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-829">如何实现将其设置为酷？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-829">How do I keep it cool?</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-830">确保电池已充电并接通电源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-830">Ensure that the battery is charged and power source is plugged in.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-831">请确保未阻止吹入或移出电脑的风扇。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-831">Make sure that the fans that blow air into or out of the PC are not blocked.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-832">在相对较酷的环境中使用 PC。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-832">Use the PC in a relatively cool environment.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-833">请确保没有热源 (例如，sun 或热通风口) PC。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-833">Make sure there are no heat sources (for example, the sun or heat vents) pointed at the PC.</span></span>

### <a name="my-visuals-are-choppy-load-slowly-or-dont-look-good"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-834">我的视觉对象不连贯、负载缓慢或外观不佳。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-834">My visuals are choppy, load slowly, or don't look good.</span></span>
