* <span data-ttu-id="79562-835">请确保将耳机插入 PC 上的正确图形卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-835">Make sure your headset is plugged into the correct graphics card on your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-836">某些 Pc 同时具有集成显卡和离散显卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-836">Some PCs have both integrated and discrete graphics cards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-837">离散卡通常会提供最佳性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-837">The discrete card will generally provide the best performance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-838">[了解有关 PC 硬件的详细信息](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-838">[Learn more about PC hardware](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-839">关闭桌面上未使用的应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-839">Close unused applications on your desktop.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-840">请确保你的头戴显示 snugly (向下移动，或者向左和向右移动以调整) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-840">Make sure your headset fits snugly (move it lower and higher or left and right to adjust).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-841">**> 混合现实 > 耳机显示** ，在 "设置" 中调整耳机的视觉设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-841">Adjust your headset's visual settings in **Settings > Mixed reality > Headset display** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-842">当 "视觉质量" 设置为 "自动" 时，我们将为你的电脑选择最佳混合现实体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-842">When "Visual quality" is set to "Automatic", we'll choose the best mixed reality experience for your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-843">若要获得更多视觉细节，请将 "视觉质量" 设置为 "高"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-843">For an experience with more visual detail, set "Visual quality" to "High".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-844">如果你的视觉对象不连贯，你可能想要选择较低的设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-844">If your visuals are choppy, you may want to select a lower setting.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-845">尝试调整头戴显示设备的校准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-845">Try adjusting your headset's calibration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-846">应对重用功能区进行调整，使之与你的 interpupillary 距离 (IPD) ，瞳孔之间的距离。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-846">The lenses should be adjusted to match your interpupillary distance (IPD), the distance between your pupils.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-847">如果你不知道 IPD，optometrist 应能够为你衡量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-847">If you don't know your IPD, an optometrist should be able to measure it for you.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-848">此外，还设计了用于度量 IPD 的网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-848">There are also websites designed to measure IPD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-849">了解 IPD 后，请使用耳机的校准旋钮进行调整。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-849">Once you know your IPD, use your headset's calibration knob to make adjustments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-850">如果耳机没有校准旋钮，请选择 " **设置" > 混合现实 > 耳机显示** 并调整 "校准控制"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-850">If the headset doesn't have a calibration knob, select **Settings > Mixed reality > Headset display** and adjust the "Calibration control".</span></span>


## <a name="tracking-system-problems"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-851">跟踪系统问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-851">Tracking system problems</span></span>

### <a name="the-system-cannot-find-the-boundary-and-im-being-presented-with-setup-ui"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-852">系统找不到边界，并显示了安装程序 UI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-852">The system cannot find the boundary and I'm being presented with setup UI.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-853">这意味着跟踪系统无法识别您的环境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-853">This means that the tracking system was unable to recognize your environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-854">如果你在新的环境中，则必须设置 [边界](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/set-up-windows-mixed-reality#set-up-your-room-boundary)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-854">If you are in a new environment, you must set up the [boundary](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/enthusiast-guide/set-up-windows-mixed-reality#set-up-your-room-boundary).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-855">如果以前在此环境中使用了该设备，并设置了边界：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-855">If you have previously used the device in this environment and set up a boundary:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-856">请确保空间充足。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-856">Make sure the room has enough light.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-857">请确保已使设备磨损，并看看房间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-857">Make sure you have worn the device and looked around the room.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-858">设备必须观察您的环境，以了解它的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-858">The device must observe your environment to know where it is.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-859">如果你的边界位于办公桌或表上，则它将找不到边界。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-859">It will not find your bounds if it is sitting on a desk or table.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-860">拔出设备，关闭 Windows Mixed Reality，并再次插入设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-860">Unplug the device, close Windows Mixed Reality, and plug the device in again.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-861">环境中的某些内容可能已更改，设备不再识别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-861">Something may have changed in your environment and the device no longer recognizes it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-862">尝试设置新边界。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-862">Try setting up a new boundary.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-863">如果这些步骤不能解决问题，请删除环境数据并再次设置边界。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-863">If these steps do not resolve the problem, then delete your environment data and set up the boundary again.</span></span>

### <a name="the-system-is-presenting-me-with-ui-that-asks-me-to-choose-setup-for-all-experiences-or-seatedstanding-and-i-see-my-bounds"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-864">系统向我提供 UI，要求我为所有经验或已安装/所有经验选择设置，并且我看到我的界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-864">The system is presenting me with UI that asks me to choose setup for all experiences or seated/standing, and I see my bounds.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-865">设备查找界限所用的时间太长。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-865">The device is taking too long to find the bounds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-866">你可以通过选择使用边界的选项来绕过此消息，并且你将在你的边界存在的情况下进入 Windows Mixed Reality 主页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-866">You can bypass this message by choosing the option to use a boundary and you will be taken to your Windows Mixed Reality Home with your bounds present.</span></span>

### <a name="i-frequently-see-a-message-saying-ive-lost-my-bounds"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-867">我经常会看到一条消息，指出 "我已经失去界限"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-867">I frequently see a message saying "I've lost my bounds".</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-868">跟踪系统正在跟踪并识别您的环境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-868">The tracking system is having a hard time tracking and identifying your environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-869">在此状态下，设备将不再显示你的边界，并且头戴式耳机切换到3DOF，使你能够在实际定位边界之前碰撞到现实世界中的东西。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-869">In this state, the device can no longer display your bounds and the headset switches to 3DOF to keep you from to bumping into things in the real world until it locates your bounds again.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-870">解决方法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-870">To fix this:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-871">请确保房间具有足够的光线。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-871">Make sure that the room has enough light.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-872">如果最近 redecorated 或重新建模房间，请重新运行安装程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-872">Rerun the setup if you recently redecorated or remodeled the room.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-873">拔出设备，关闭 Windows Mixed Reality，并再次将其插入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-873">Unplug the device, close Windows Mixed Reality, and plug it in again.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-874">清除环境数据并再次设置设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-874">Clear your environment data and set up the device again.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="79562-875">如果消息仍然存在，请与客户支持联系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-875">If the message persists, contact customer support.</span></span>

### <a name="i-can-look-around-but-i-cant-translate-im-stuck-in-3dof"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-876">我可以找出，但无法转换 (我在 3DOF) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-876">I can look around but I can't translate (I'm stuck in 3DOF).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-877">这意味着跟踪系统无法生成姿势，或应用程序已停止使用新的姿势数据来呈现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-877">This means that the tracking system cannot generate pose, or the application has stopped using new pose data to render.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-878">检查下列项目：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-878">Check the following:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-879">请确保空间充足。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-879">Make sure the room has enough light.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-880">请确保会议室有足够的详细信息可供跟踪。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-880">Make sure the room has enough details to track.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-881">拔出设备，关闭 Windows Mixed Reality，并再次插入设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-881">Unplug the device, close Windows Mixed Reality, and plug in the device again.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-882">如果消息仍然存在，请联系客户支持部门</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-882">If the message persists, contact customer support</span></span>

### <a name="the-view-in-the-hmd-is-completely-frozen"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-883">HMD 中的视图被完全冻结。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-883">The view in the HMD is completely frozen.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-884">这通常意味着应用程序或系统级组件发生了故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-884">This usually means the application or a system level component has failed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-885">尝试执行以下操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-885">Try to:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-886">按 "home" 按钮退出应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-886">Press the "home" button to leave the application.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-887">拔出设备，关闭 MRP 并重新插回设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-887">Unplug the device, close MRP and plug the device back in.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-888">重启电脑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-888">Reboot the PC.</span></span>

### <a name="i-frequently-see-a-black-border-around-the-edges-of-the-view-in-the-hmd-sometimes-it-looks-like-im-looking-down-a-tunnel"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-889">我经常在 HMD 的视图边缘周围看到黑色边框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-889">I frequently see a black border around the edges of the view in the HMD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-890">有时，似乎正在按下一个隧道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-890">Sometimes it looks like I'm looking down a tunnel.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-891">这意味着应用程序不能在您的 PC 上击中帧速率，系统使用旧帧在 HMD 中呈现视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-891">This means that the application is not able to hit frame rate on your PC and the system is using old frames to render the view in the HMD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-892">由于应用程序仅呈现您正在查看的世界部分，因此，如果这些应用程序不一直达到帧速率，则系统将尝试继续从以前的视图开始渲染世界，并使用黑色填充缺少的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-892">Since applications only render the part of the world you are looking at, if they do not consistently hit their frame rates, then the system will attempt to continue to render the world from a previous point of view and will fill in the missing details with black.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-893">如果经常发生这种情况：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-893">If this happens frequently:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-894">关闭或终止所有不需要的程序以释放内存和 CPU。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-894">Close or terminate all unneeded programs to free up memory and CPU.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-895">减少应用程序中的详细信息设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-895">Reduce detail settings in your application.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-896">减小 Windows Mixed Reality 设置中的详细信息设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-896">Reduce detail settings in Windows Mixed Reality settings.</span></span>

### <a name="the-view-in-the-hmd-is-jittering-and-stuttering-a-lot"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-897">HMD 中的视图是 jittering 和断断续续。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-897">The view in the HMD is jittering and stuttering a lot.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-898">出现这种情况的原因有多种。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-898">There are several reasons this may happen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-899">主要原因是系统无法将内容呈现给耳机，或者跟踪系统遇到问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-899">The primary causes are the system not being able to render content to the headset, or the tracking system is experiencing problems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-900">检查下列项目：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-900">Check the following:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-901">请确保您的 PC 不受资源争用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-901">Make sure your PC is not under resource contention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-902">打开任务管理器并确保计算资源是免费的 (例如，80% CPU free，ram 和磁盘 IO 的400MB 低于 80% ) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-902">Open Task Manager and ensure your compute resources are free (for example, 80% CPU free, 400MB of ram and disk IO is below 80%).</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-903">请确保你具有适用于你的硬件的最新图形驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-903">Make sure you have the latest graphics drivers for your hardware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-904">有关详细信息，请参阅图形驱动程序部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-904">See the graphics driver section for more info.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-905">请确保空间充足。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-905">Make sure the room has enough light.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-906">拔出设备，关闭 Windows Mixed Reality，并再次插入设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-906">Unplug the device, close Windows Mixed Reality, and plug the device in again.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="79562-907">重启你的计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-907">Reboot your PC.</span></span>
6. <span data-ttu-id="79562-908">如果问题仍然存在，请与客户支持联系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-908">If the problem persists, contact customer support.</span></span>

### <a name="the-world-briefly-froze-and-perhaps-tilted-or-flipped-upside-before-returning-to-normal"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-909">在返回到 normal 之前，世界上的冻结，可能会短暂地倾斜或翻转。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-909">The world briefly froze and perhaps tilted or flipped upside before returning to normal.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-910">这可能是由于应用或系统级别组件出现严重错误，或者暂时缺少内存或 CPU 资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-910">This could be caused by an app or system level component hitting a fatal error, or a temporary lack of memory or CPU resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-911">检查下列项目：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-911">Check the following:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-912">打开 "任务管理器"，确保至少有20% 的 CPU 可用内存和400MB 内存可用 (例如，80% CPU 可用空间，ram 和磁盘 IO 的400MB 低于 80% ) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-912">Open "Task Manager" and ensure you have at least 20% CPU free and 400MB memory free (e.g. 80% CPU free, 400MB of ram and disk IO is below 80%).</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-913">打开 "事件查看器"，并在冻结时间附近，跳到 " **Windows 日志" > 应用程序和错误** 事件项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-913">Open "Event Viewer" and go to **Windows Logs > Application and Error** event entries around the time of the freeze.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-914">检查是否有任何进程崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-914">Check to see if any processes crashed.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-915">如果此问题仍然存在，请尝试重启电脑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-915">Try rebooting the PC if this problem persists.</span></span>

### <a name="the-world-flipped-upside-down-momentarily-and-returned-to-normal"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-916">世界翻转并返回到正常状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-916">The world flipped upside down momentarily and returned to normal.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-917">这通常是由于从耳机获取传感器数据以通知跟踪算法时出错引起的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-917">This is typically caused by errors in obtaining sensor data from the headset to inform the tracking algorithms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-918">如果经常发生这种情况：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-918">If this happens frequently:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-919">将耳机插入到其他 USB 3.0 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-919">Plug the headset into a different USB 3.0 port.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-920">将耳机直接插入 PC，而不是 USB 3.0 集线器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-920">Plug the headset directly into the PC rather than a USB 3.0 hub.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-921">如果问题仍然存在，请与客户支持联系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-921">If the problem persists, contact customer support.</span></span>

### <a name="the-world-is-tilted-but-i-can-navigate-and-walk-around-fine-in-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-922">世界是倾斜的，但我可以在 Windows Mixed Reality 中进行导航和演练。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-922">The world is tilted but I can navigate and walk around fine in Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-923">这通常是由将传感器数据错误记录到电脑上存储的环境数据中引起的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-923">This is usually caused by sensor data errors being recorded into the environment data that is stored on your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-924">这可能会导致 Windows Mixed Reality 显示为倾斜，有时会永久显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-924">This can cause the Windows Mixed Reality to appear tilted, sometimes permanently.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-925">请尝试以下做法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-925">Try the following:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-926">拔下 HMD，关闭 Windows Mixed Reality 并插上耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-926">Unplug the HMD, close Windows Mixed Reality and plug the headset back in.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-927">重启电脑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-927">Reboot the PC.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-928">清除你的环境数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-928">Clear your environment data.</span></span>

## <a name="webvr-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-929">WebVR 问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-929">WebVR questions</span></span>

### <a name="why-cant-i-see-my-controllers-when-viewing-vr-content-from-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-930">从边缘查看 VR 内容时为什么看不到我的控制器？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-930">Why can’t I see my controllers when viewing VR content from Edge?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-931">并非所有 WebVR 内容都是为支持运动控制器而编写的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-931">Not all WebVR content is authored to support motion controllers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-932">WebVR 允许内容开发人员支持不同类型的输入，例如游戏控制器或运动控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-932">WebVR allows developers of content to support different types of input, such as game controllers or motion controllers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-933">如果你在站点上看不到控制器，则它可能不支持移动控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-933">If you do not see your controllers on a site, it likely doesn’t have motion controller support.</span></span>

### <a name="why-cant-i-use-the-mouse-in-an-immersive-webvr-view"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-934">为什么无法在沉浸式 WebVR 视图中使用鼠标？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-934">Why can't I use the mouse in an immersive WebVR view?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-935">这是 WebVR 规范的一项可选功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-935">This is an optional feature of the WebVR specification.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-936">并非所有浏览器都支持此功能，并且并不是所有的 WebVR 内容都是为了支持鼠标输入而编写的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-936">Not all browsers support this feature, and not all WebVR content is authored to support mouse input.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-937">WebVR 允许内容开发人员支持不同类型的输入，例如鼠标、键盘、游戏控制器或运动控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-937">WebVR allows content developers to support different types of input, such as mouse, keyboard, game controllers or motion controllers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-938">鼠标输入行为因浏览器而异。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-938">Mouse input behavior varies per browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-939">在 Microsoft Edge 中，网站作者必须确保在向耳机提供时使用 "pointerlock" 才能正常工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-939">Within Microsoft Edge, website authors must ensure they take 'pointerlock' when presenting to the headset for mouse input to work.</span></span>

### <a name="why-does-my-controller-look-like-a-viveoculus-has-strange-orientation-or-the-buttons-are-incorrectly-mapped"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-940">为什么控制器看上去类似于 Naopak/Oculus，有奇怪的方向，或按钮映射不正确？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-940">Why does my controller look like a Vive/Oculus, has strange orientation, or the buttons are incorrectly mapped?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-941">该网站可能没有完全的动作控制器支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-941">The website likely doesn’t have full motion controller support.</span></span>

### <a name="why-cant-i-view-360-degree-videos-from-youtubefacebookvimeothe-guardiannew-york-times-etc-from-edge-in-vr"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-942">为什么我不能从 Youtube/Facebook/Vimeo/监护人/纽约时间等中查看360学位视频？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-942">Why can’t I view 360 degree videos from Youtube/Facebook/Vimeo/The Guardian/New York Times, etc. from Edge in VR?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-943">就像任何其他 web 规范或标准一样，作者也可以选择实现它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-943">Just like any other web specification or standard, the author has the choice to implement it or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-944">WebVR 规范允许网站直接从浏览器启动 VR 体验，这些网站的作者目前尚未实现此规范。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-944">There is a WebVR specification that allows websites to launch VR experiences directly from the browser and the authors of these websites have not implemented this specification at this time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-945">在某些平台上，可以使用可下载的应用来查看这些供应商的 VR 内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-945">There may be downloadable apps on some platforms that enable viewing of VR content from these vendors.</span></span>

### <a name="why-cant-i-enter-vr-from-firefox-or-chrome"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-946">为什么无法从 Firefox 或 Chrome 进入 VR？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-946">Why can’t I enter VR from Firefox or Chrome?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-947">目前，Windows Mixed Reality 设备目前仅支持 WebVR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-947">WebVR is only supported by Windows Mixed Reality devices in Edge at this time.</span></span>

### <a name="when-i-enter-vr-from-a-website-why-do-i-see-a-blank-screen-in-my-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-948">当我从网站输入 "VR" 时，为什么我在我的耳机中看到了空白屏幕？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-948">When I enter VR from a website, why do I see a blank screen in my headset?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-949">网站可能未实现对多 GPU 计算机的支持 (包括混合 GPU 便携式计算机) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-949">The website may not have implemented support for Multi GPU machines (including Hybrid GPU laptops).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-950">尝试执行以下操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-950">Try to:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-951">重载页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-951">Reload the page.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-952">在台式计算机上，将耳机插入与显示 Microsoft Edge 的监视器相同的图形适配器中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-952">On desktop machines, plug the headset into the same graphics adapter as the monitor that is displaying Microsoft Edge.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-953">将两者插到更高的显卡，而不是集成图形适配器中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-953">Plug both into the higher powered graphics card, not into the integrated graphics adapter.</span></span>

### <a name="when-i-exit-vr-when-watching-a-video-from-edge-the-sound-continues-playing-but-the-edge-window-is-grayed-out"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-954">当我在观看从边缘观看视频时退出 VR 时，声音将继续播放，但边缘窗口灰显。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-954">When I exit VR when watching a video from Edge, the sound continues playing but the Edge window is grayed out.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-955">这是在混合现实 cliffhouse 中从边缘运行 WebVR 时的已知问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-955">This is a known issue when running WebVR from Edge in the Mixed Reality cliffhouse.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-956">若要解决此问题，请按键盘上的 esc 键，而不是按 windows 按钮退出 WebVR 体验，或通过选择并停止视频来激活灰显边缘窗口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-956">To resolve it, press escape on the keyboard rather than pressing the windows button to exit the WebVR experience, or activate the greyed out Edge window by selecting it and then stop the video.</span></span>

### <a name="can-i-use-webvr-on-the-hololens"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-957">能否在 HoloLens 上使用 WebVR？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-957">Can I use WebVR on the HoloLens?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-958">Microsoft 目前还没有在 HoloLens 上公布有关 WebVR 的任何信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-958">Microsoft has not announced anything about WebVR on the HoloLens at this point.</span></span>

### <a name="why-is-my-view-at-floor-level-when-viewing-webvr-content-from-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-959">从边缘查看 WebVR 内容时，为什么我的视图处于地面级别？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-959">Why is my view at floor level when viewing WebVR content from Edge?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-960">网站未正确支持 Windows Mixed Reality 耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-960">The website does not properly support Windows Mixed Reality headsets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-961">要解决此问题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-961">To work around this:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-962">将耳机置于空间的基底。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-962">Place the headset on the floor of your space.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-963">使用 Microsoft Edge 在桌面上导航到 WebVR 页面， (不在混合现实) 内。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-963">Navigate to the WebVR page using Microsoft Edge on your desktop (not within Mixed Reality).</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-964">单击网页上的按钮进入 "VR"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-964">Click the button on the webpage to Enter VR.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-965">请等待5-10 秒钟，让体验完全进入沉浸式模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-965">Wait 5-10 seconds for the experience to fully enter immersive mode.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="79562-966">拿起耳机，将其放在您的头上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-966">Pick up the headset and place it on your head.</span></span>

### <a name="the-display-is-very-low-resolution-in-some-webvr-experiences"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-967">在某些 WebVR 体验中，显示器的分辨率非常低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-967">The display is very low resolution in some WebVR experiences.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-968">网站未正确支持高分辨率耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-968">The websites do not properly support high resolution headsets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-969">解决方法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-969">To workaround this:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-970">如果从桌面 (而不是从混合现实 cliffhouse) 中启动 WebVR，请在进入 VR 之前确保窗口最大化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-970">If launching WebVR from the desktop (as opposed to from within the Mixed Reality cliffhouse), ensure the window is maximized prior to Entering VR.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-971">输入 VR 后，请避免调整 Microsoft Edge 窗口的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-971">Avoid resizing the Microsoft Edge window after you have entered VR.</span></span>

### <a name="why-does-the-webvr-immersive-view-exit-when-i-change-browser-tabs"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-972">为什么当我更改浏览器选项卡时，WebVR 沉浸式视图退出？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-972">Why does the WebVR immersive view exit when I change browser tabs?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-973">这是预期的行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-973">This is expected behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-974">出于安全原因，只有活动的浏览器选项卡可以访问连接的耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-974">For security reasons, only the active browser tab can access connected headsets.</span></span>

### <a name="why-cant-i-hear-audio-on-a-particular-webvr-experience"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-975">为什么听不到特定 WebVR 体验的音频？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-975">Why can't I hear audio on a particular WebVR experience?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-976">网站可能使用的是 Microsoft Edge 当前不支持的 OGG 音频文件格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-976">The website may be using the OGG audio file format, which Microsoft Edge does not currently support.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-977">你可以在 [问题跟踪](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-edge/platform/issues/)程序中直接向 Microsoft Edge 浏览器团队报告断开的网站，也可以通过 twitter 使用 [#EdgeBug 井号标签](https://blogs.windows.com/msedgedev/2016/08/11/edgebug-twitter/)来向其报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-977">You can report broken sites directly to the Microsoft Edge browser team in the [issue tracker](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-edge/platform/issues/), or via twitter using [#EdgeBug hashtag](https://blogs.windows.com/msedgedev/2016/08/11/edgebug-twitter/).</span></span>

### <a name="why-does-haptic-feedback-not-work-in-webvr-with-motion-controllers"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-978">为什么 Haptic 的反馈在 WebVR 中不能与运动控制器一起使用？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-978">Why does Haptic feedback not work in WebVR with motion controllers?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-979">Microsoft Edge 目前不支持 WebVR 游戏板 API 扩展上的 haptics。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-979">Microsoft Edge does not currently support haptics on the WebVR gamepad API extensions.</span></span>


## <a name="steamvr-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-980">SteamVR 问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-980">SteamVR questions</span></span>

### <a name="how-can-i-play-steamvr-games-in-my-windows-mixed-reality-immersive-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-981">如何在 Windows Mixed Reality 沉浸式耳机上播放 SteamVR 游戏？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-981">How can I play SteamVR games in my Windows Mixed Reality immersive headset?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-982">你必须在你的电脑上安装适用于 SteamVR 的 Windows Mixed Reality 并设置 SteamVR：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-982">You must install Windows Mixed Reality for SteamVR on your PC and set up SteamVR:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-983">[下载并安装 SteamVR](https://steamcdn-a.akamaihd.net/client/installer/SteamWindowsMRInstaller.exe)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-983">[Download and install SteamVR](https://steamcdn-a.akamaihd.net/client/installer/SteamWindowsMRInstaller.exe).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-984">启动 SteamVR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-984">Start SteamVR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-985">SteamVR 教程应该会自动启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-985">The SteamVR Tutorial should start automatically.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-986">将耳机连接到电脑，并打开运动控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-986">Connect your headset to your PC and turn on your motion controllers.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-987">加载 Windows Mixed Reality 主页并显示控制器后，请在桌面上打开流应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-987">Once the Windows Mixed Reality home has loaded and your controllers are visible, open the Steam app on your desktop.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-988">使用流应用从您的流库中启动 SteamVR 游戏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-988">Use the Steam app to launch a SteamVR game from your Steam library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-989">若要在不停用耳机的情况下启动 SteamVR 游戏，可以在 Windows Mixed Reality 的 " **开始" > 所有应用** 中找到并启动它们。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-989">To launch SteamVR games without taking off your headset, you can find and launch them under Windows Mixed Reality's **Start > All Apps** .</span></span> 

### <a name="i-get-a-message-that-says-to-use-steamvr-with-windows-mixed-reality-you-need-to-install-the-latest-windows-update-or-windows-developer-mode-required"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-990">我收到一条消息，显示 "要将 SteamVR 与 Windows Mixed Reality 一起使用"，则需要安装最新的 Windows 更新 "或" 必需的 Windows 开发人员模式 "。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-990">I get a message that says “To use SteamVR with Windows Mixed Reality, you need to install the latest Windows Update" or "Windows Developer Mode Required".</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-991">确保你的计算机运行的是最新版本的 Windows 10。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-991">Make sure your PC is running the latest version of Windows 10.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-992">若要查看此信息，请参阅 " **设置" > 系统 > 关于** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-992">To check this, go to **Settings  > System > About** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-993">在 "Windows 规范" 下，确保 "OS Build" 为16299.64 或更高版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-993">Under "Windows specifications", make sure "OS Build" is 16299.64 or greater.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-994">请确保没有任何等待下载或安装的更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-994">Make sure you don’t have any updates waiting to download or install.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-995">请参阅 " **设置" > 更新 & 安全 > Windows 更新** ，然后选择 "检查更新"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-995">Go to **Settings  > Update & Security > Windows Update** and select "Check for updates".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-996">可能需要多次检查更新，以便继续检查更新，直到没有更多更新可用，然后重启电脑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-996">You may have to check for updates multiple times so keep checking for updates until no further updates are available and then restart your PC.</span></span>

### <a name="steamvr-is-crashing-after-updating-windows"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-997">更新 Windows 后，SteamVR 崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-997">SteamVR is crashing after updating Windows.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-998">SteamVR 的某些较旧版本的 Windows Mixed Reality 不再与 Windows 兼容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-998">Some older versions of Windows Mixed Reality for SteamVR are no longer compatible with Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-999">对于 SteamVR，可能有旧版本的 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-999">You may have an old version of Windows Mixed Reality for SteamVR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1000">若要确保你是最新的：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1000">To ensure that you are up to date:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1001">在您的流库中，请参阅 **软件 > Windows Mixed Reality For SteamVR** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1001">In your Steam library, go to **Software > Windows Mixed Reality for SteamVR** .</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1002">右键单击它并跳到 "属性"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1002">Right click it and go to "Properties".</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1003">选择 "更新" 选项卡，然后选择 "始终保持此应用程序最新"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1003">Select the "Update" tab and select "Always keep this application up to date".</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1004">转到 "本地文件" 选项卡，然后选择 "验证应用程序文件的完整性" 来强制更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1004">Force the update by going to the "Local Files" tab and selecting “Verify integrity of application files”.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1005">重新启动流和 SteamVR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1005">Restart Steam and SteamVR.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1006">如果在更新后 SteamVR 仍崩溃，则可能会在计算机上为 SteamVR 安装两个 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1006">If SteamVR is still crashing after updating you may have two installations of Windows Mixed Reality for SteamVR on your machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1007">若要确认是否属于这种情况：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1007">To confirm if this is the case:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1008">找到%localappdata%\openvr\openvrpaths.vrpath 并在记事本中打开它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1008">Locate %localappdata%\openvr\openvrpaths.vrpath and open it in Notepad.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1009">在 "外部驱动程序" 部分，查找 "MixedRealityVRDriver" 的多个条目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1009">Under the "external drivers" sections look for multiple entries for "MixedRealityVRDriver"</span></span> 
   ```json
   "external_drivers" : [
      "D:\\Steam\\steamapps\\common\\MixedRealityVRDriver",
      "E:\\Steam\\steamapps\\common\\MixedRealityVRDriver"
   ],
   ```
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1010">如果看到多个条目，请删除这两个条目中较早的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1010">If you see multiple entries, remove the older of the two entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1011">请注意，如果只有一个条目，则行末尾不应再有逗号，例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1011">Note that once you have only one entry there should no longer be a comma at the end of the line, for example:</span></span>
   ```json
   "external_drivers" : [
      "D:\\Steam\\steamapps\\common\\MixedRealityVRDriver"
   ],
   ```
4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1012">保存文件并将其关闭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1012">Save the file and close it.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1013">重新启动流和 SteamVR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1013">Restart Steam and SteamVR.</span></span>

### <a name="my-controllers-arent-working-as-expected-in-steamvr"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1014">我的控制器在 SteamVR 中不能按预期方式工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1014">My controllers aren't working as expected in SteamVR.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1015">关闭 SteamVR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1015">Close SteamVR.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1016">返回到混合现实回家，确认控制器正在按预期方式工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1016">Return to the Mixed Reality Home and confirm that your controllers are working as expected.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1017">再次启动 SteamVR 体验，控制器应恢复正常。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1017">Launch the SteamVR experience again and your controllers should be back to normal.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1018">如果问题仍然存在，请使用 [Windows 反馈中心](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4021566/windows-10-send-feedback-to-microsoft-with-feedback-hub-app) 在混合现实类别下提供反馈，并在摘要中包括 SteamVR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1018">If issues persist please file feedback using the [Windows Feedback Hub](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4021566/windows-10-send-feedback-to-microsoft-with-feedback-hub-app) under the Mixed Reality category and include SteamVR in the summary.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1019">请注意，在不同的游戏中，你将以不同的方式使用移动控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1019">Note that you'll use your motion controllers differently in different games.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1020">下面是一些可帮助你入门的基础知识：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1020">Here are a few basics to help you get started:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1021">若要打开 "流" 仪表板，请在左侧操纵杆上按 "向下"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1021">To open the Steam dashboard, press straight down on the left thumbstick.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1022">若要退出 SteamVR 游戏并返回到 Windows Mixed Reality 主页，请按 Windows 按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1022">To exit a SteamVR game and return to the Windows Mixed Reality home, press the Windows button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1023">然后选择屏幕上显示的混合现实主页按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1023">Then select the Mixed Reality Home button that appears on screen.</span></span>

### <a name="my-left-and-right-controllers-are-reversed-in-steamvr"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1024">在 SteamVR 中，我的左控制器和右控制器反转。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1024">My left and right controllers are reversed in SteamVR.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1025">关闭控制器并将其左移，然后将其左移一，然后将其打开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1025">Start the game with your controllers off and then turn the left one on, followed by the right one.</span></span>

### <a name="my-games-are-running-slowly"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1026">游戏运行速度缓慢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1026">My games are running slowly.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1027">确认你的电脑满足 Windows Mixed Reality 中 SteamVR 的规范</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1027">Confirm that your PC meets the specifications for SteamVR in Windows Mixed Reality</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1028">确认你的电脑满足你正在播放的 SteamVR 游戏的规格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1028">Confirm that your PC meets the specifications for the SteamVR game you are playing.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1029">在桌面上的混合现实门户中，选择 "暂停" 停止桌面预览。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1029">In Mixed Reality Portal on your desktop, select "Pause" to stop desktop preview.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1030">按照上述说明确保你运行的是 Windows 10 内部版本16299.64 或更高版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1030">Follow the instructions above to make sure you are running Windows 10 build 16299.64 or later.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1031">请确保您的 PC 具有最新的图形驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1031">Make sure your PC has the latest graphics drivers.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1032">检查任务管理器以查看您的计算机上可能正在运行的其他进程并使用资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1032">Check Task Manager to see what other processes might be running on your PC and consuming resources.</span></span>
6. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1033">检查流是否正在后台下载游戏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1033">Check to see if Steam is downloading a game in the background.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1034">这可能会消耗资源并使游戏运行不佳。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1034">This can consume resources and make games run poorly.</span></span>
7. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1035">存在一个已知的性能问题，它会影响一小类不具有可见窗口的应用程序，例如 SteamVR Home。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1035">There is a known performance issue that affects a small class of apps that do not have a visible window, for example, SteamVR Home.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1036">大多数应用不属于此类别，并且在将来的更新中会提供修补程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1036">The vast majority of apps do not fall into this category, and a fix will be available in a future update.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1037">如果仍遇到意外性能问题，请使用 Windows 反馈中心向我们发送反馈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1037">If you're still running into unexpected performance issues, please send us feedback using the Windows Feedback Hub.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1038">请确保按照说明操作以 [包含 SteamVR 性能跟踪](using-steamvr-with-windows-mixed-reality.md#sharing-feedback-on-steamvr)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1038">Make sure to follow the instructions to [include a SteamVR Performance Trace](using-steamvr-with-windows-mixed-reality.md#sharing-feedback-on-steamvr).</span></span> 

### <a name="steamvr-is-showing-a-compositor-error-for-example-shared-ipc-compositor-connect-failed-400"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1039">SteamVR 显示了一个组合器错误 (例如，"Shared IPC 合成器 Connect Failed (400) " ) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1039">SteamVR is showing a compositor error (for example, "Shared IPC Compositor Connect Failed (400)").</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1040">存在一个已知问题，如果头戴显示在两个不同的视频适配器上，可能会发生这种情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1040">There is a known issue where this can happen if your headset and primary monitor are on two different video adapters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1041">将监视器连接到与耳机相同的适配器，并将该监视器配置为 "设置" 应用中的主监视器 **> 系统 > 显示** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1041">Attach your monitor to the same adapter as your headset and configure that monitor to be the primary monitor in **Settings app > System > Display** .</span></span>

### <a name="steamvr-content-appears-in-the-wrong-place-like-beneath-the-floor-or-above-my-head"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1042">SteamVR 内容显示在错误的位置，例如，位于其下的地面或上方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1042">SteamVR content appears in the wrong place, like beneath the floor or above my head.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1043">重置位置：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1043">Reset your position:</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1044">单击左侧控制器的操纵杆，打开 "SteamVR 仪表板"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1044">Click the left controller's thumbstick to bring up the "SteamVR Dashboard".</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1045">选择 "设置" 按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1045">Select the "Settings" button.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1046">选择 "重置固定位置"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1046">Select "Reset Seated Position".</span></span>

### <a name="my-steam-app-closed-unexpectedly"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1047">我的流应用意外关闭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1047">My Steam app closed unexpectedly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1048">如果你锁定电脑屏幕、删除头戴显示设备、切换用户或电脑进入睡眠状态，则流应用将关闭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1048">The Steam app will close if you lock your PC screen, remove your headset, switch users, or if your PC goes to sleep.</span></span>


## <a name="speech-and-audio-problems"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1049">语音和音频问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1049">Speech and audio problems</span></span>

### <a name="i-cant-hear-any-sound-in-my-headset-or-sound-is-playing-through-my-computer-instead-of-my-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1050">我在我的耳机中听不到任何声音，或通过我的计算机而不是我的耳机播放声音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1050">I can't hear any sound in my headset, or sound is playing through my computer instead of my headset.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1051">如果沉浸式耳机不包含内置耳机，则需要将耳机连接到耳机上的音频插孔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1051">If your immersive headset doesn’t include built-in headphones, you’ll need to connect headphones to the audio jack on the headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1052">插孔通常位于耳机面板或重用功能区的后面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1052">The jack is often located just behind or under the headset visor or lenses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1053">如果找不到，请与你的耳机制造商联系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1053">Check with your headset manufacturer if you can't find it.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1054">某些音频耳机有物理按钮来控制音量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1054">Some audio headsets have physical buttons to control the volume.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1055">如果音频不起作用，请检查卷是否已关闭或静音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1055">If audio isn't working, check to see whether the volume is turned down or muted.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1056">Windows Mixed Reality 旨在在混合现实门户运行时通过沉浸式耳机播放声音，并已将耳机连接到该门户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1056">Windows Mixed Reality is designed to play sound through your immersive headset when the Mixed Reality Portal is running and you have headphones connected to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1057">当你离开或翻转面板时，请关闭混合现实门户应用程序，或在15分钟内未使用该应用程序时，音频将切换到默认的 Windows 播放设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1057">When you take the headset off or flip the visor up, close the Mixed Reality Portal application, or when that app has not been used for 15 minutes, audio will switch to your default Windows playback device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1058">你可以在 "设置" 中更改此设置 **> 混合现实 > 音频和语音。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1058">You can change this setting in **Settings > Mixed reality > Audio and speech.**</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1059">请确保将音频耳机完全插入音频插孔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1059">Make sure your audio headset is plugged into the audio jack completely.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1060">特别要注意的是，Acer 耳机可能需要更多的警惕，以确保音频耳机始终处于插接方向。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1060">The Acer headset in particular may require more care to ensure the audio headset is plugged in all the way.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1061">检查音频耳机/麦克风是否已插入耳机，而不是计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1061">Check that the audio headset/microphone is plugged into the headset and not the PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1062">Windows 声音控制面板只显示已启用的音频终结点，而不是已禁用的终结点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1062">The Windows Sound Control Panel only shows enabled audio endpoints, not disabled endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1063">当你不戴上耳机时，耳机音频设备将被禁用，因此你必须在 "声音控制面板" 中右键单击，然后选择 "显示已禁用的设备" 进行查看;设备名称为 "Realtek USB 2.0 音频"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1063">The headset audio device will be disabled when you're not wearing the headset, so you have to right-click in the sound control panel and choose "Show disabled devices" to see it; the device name is "Realtek USB2.0 Audio".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1064">完成此操作后，可以将 "属性" 页中的名称更改为更容易识别的内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1064">Once you do this, you can change the name in the "Properties" page to something you'll recognize more easily.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1065">可以为播放和录制选项卡执行此操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1065">You can do this for both the playback and recording tabs.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1066">如果音频在混合现实应用中不工作 (例如，Netflix) ，则这可能是由于已知问题导致的，该问题不会自动更新 Windows Mixed Reality 来匹配操作系统版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1066">If your audio is not working in Mixed Reality apps (for example, Netflix), this may be caused by a known issue where Windows Mixed Reality is not be automatically updated to match the OS version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1067">若要解决此问题并获得最佳混合现实体验，请转到 " **设置" > 更新 & 安全 > Windows 更新 > 检查是否有更新** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1067">To fix this issue and get the best Mixed Reality experience, go to **Settings > Update & Security > Windows Update > Check for Updates** .</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1068">**注意：** Windows Mixed Reality 空间音频最适合用于直接内置或直接连接到沉浸式耳机的耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1068">**Note:** Windows Mixed Reality spatial audio works best with headphones built into or connected directly to your immersive headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1069">连接到 PC 的 PC 扬声器或耳机可能不适用于空间音频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1069">PC speakers or headphones connected to the PC might not work well for spatial audio.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1070">**注意：** Windows Mixed Reality 不支持蓝牙音频耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1070">**Note:** Windows Mixed Reality doesn’t support Bluetooth audio headsets.</span></span>

### <a name="im-experiencing-sudden-volume-changes-lost-audio-or-buzzing"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1071">我遇到了突然发生的变化、音频丢失或嗡嗡声。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1071">I'm experiencing sudden volume changes, lost audio, or buzzing.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1072">某些应用程序（包括许多通过 SteamVR 启动的应用程序）可能会在音频设备随着你开始或停止混合现实门户而发生变化时丢失音频或挂起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1072">Some applications, including many of those launched through SteamVR, can lose audio or hang when the audio device changes as you start or stop the Mixed Reality Portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1073">打开混合现实门户应用以更正此错误后，请重新启动应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1073">Restart the app after you have opened the Mixed Reality Portal app to correct this.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1074">如果另一台多媒体 USB 设备 (如 web cam) 与 Windows Mixed Reality 耳机共享同一内部或外部 USB 集线器，则耳机音频插孔/耳机可能会偶尔发出声音或根本没有音频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1074">If another multimedia USB device (such as a web cam) shares the same internal or external USB hub with the Windows Mixed Reality headset, the headset's audio jack/headphones may occasionally have a buzzing sound or no audio at all.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1075">将耳机插入使用不同集线器的 USB 端口，或断开连接/禁用其他 USB 多媒体设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1075">Plug your headset into a USB port that uses a different hub or disconnect/disable your other USB multimedia device.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1076">如果你注意到耳机上连接了耳机的噪音太大，则可能是电脑的 USB 集线器无法为 Windows Mixed Reality 耳机提供足够的电源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1076">If you notice a loud burst of noise from headphones connected to the headset, it is possible that the PC's USB hub is not able to provide enough power to the Windows Mixed Reality headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1077">如果发生这种情况，请立即提交 [反馈中心](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-feedback) bug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1077">If this occurs, file a [Feedback Hub](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-feedback) bug immediately.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1078">解决方法有助于不使用扩展电缆，使用专用的外部电源 USB 3.0 集线器，或尝试在电脑上使用其他 USB 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1078">Workarounds that may help include not using extension cables, using a dedicated, external powered USB 3.0 HUB, or trying a different USB port on the PC.</span></span>

### <a name="my-bluetooth-audio-headset-isnt-working-as-expected"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1079">我的蓝牙音频耳机未按预期工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1079">My Bluetooth audio headset isn't working as expected.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1080">Microsoft 不建议将蓝牙音频耳机用于 Windows Mixed Reality。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1080">Microsoft does not recommend using Bluetooth audio headsets with Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1081">蓝牙音频外设不适用于 Windows Mixed Reality 声音和空间音效，蓝牙音频耳机无法同时支持麦克风输入和立体声输出，因此，在使用 gamechat 或其他语音输入时，您不会听到立体声或 spatialized 声音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1081">Bluetooth audio peripherals do not work well with Windows Mixed Reality voice and spatial sound experiences, and Bluetooth audio headsets cannot support microphone input and stereo output at the same time, so you won't hear stereo or spatialized sound when using it for gamechat or other voice input.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1082">蓝牙音频耳机还会对运动控制器体验产生负面影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1082">Bluetooth audio headsets can also negatively affect your motion controller experience.</span></span> 

### <a name="sound-isnt-coming-from-expected-directions"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1083">声音并非来自预期方向。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1083">Sound isn't coming from expected directions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1084">Windows Mixed Reality 主页包含的空间音质 (音频，这听起来像是来自家庭) 的应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1084">The Windows Mixed Reality home includes spatial sound (audio that sounds like it comes from the apps located in your home).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1085">当您从每个应用程序中翻到更近或更远的距离时，声音方向和级别会改变以使真实感更进一步。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1085">As you turn around and move closer or farther from each app, the sound direction and level will change to further the sense of realism.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1086">下面是意外声音方向的一些原因：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1086">Here are some reasons for unexpected sound directions:</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1087">当你在家中打开并播放支持后台的音乐应用的音乐时 (例如，在家庭中) Groove 音乐，然后 (像游戏) 那样打开沉浸式的</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1087">When you open and play music from a background-capable music app (like Groove Music) in your home and then open an immersive VR experience (like a game), the sound from the music app will crossfade from spatial sound to stereo.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1088">它的显示时间可能大于之前，因为您与声音之间没有任何距离。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1088">It may appear louder than before because there is no longer any distance between you and the sound.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1089">如果在使用 Windows Mixed Reality 耳机之前已在主机 PC 上启用 Cortana，则可能会丢失适用于 Windows Mixed Reality 主页中的应用的空间声音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1089">If you had Cortana enabled on your host PC prior to using your Windows Mixed Reality headset, you may lose the spatial sound applied to the apps in your Windows Mixed Reality home.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1090">若要解决此问题，请在启动 Windows Mixed Reality 之前，在桌面的 "设置" 中将 "允许 Cortana 响应你好小娜" **> 设置** 为 "Sonic"，或者在 Windows mixed reality 主页的 "桌面应用" 窗口中启用 "Windows for 耳机"：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1090">To fix this, either turn off "Let Cortana respond to Hey Cortana" in **Settings > Cortana** on your desktop before launching Windows Mixed Reality, or enable "Windows Sonic for Headphones" from within the Desktop app window in Windows Mixed Reality home:</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1091">在桌面任务栏上左键单击扬声器图标，并从音频设备列表中选择它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1091">Left-click the speaker icon on the desktop taskbar and select it from the list of audio devices.</span></span>
    2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1092">右键单击桌面任务栏上的扬声器图标，然后在 "扬声器设置" 菜单中选择 "Windows Sonic 用于耳机"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1092">Right-click the speaker icon on the desktop taskbar and select "Windows Sonic for Headphones" in the "Speaker setup" menu.</span></span>
    3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1093">为所有音频设备重复以下步骤， (终结点) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1093">Repeat these steps for all of your audio devices (endpoints).</span></span>

### <a name="speech-commands-are-not-working-as-expected"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1094">语音命令未按预期方式工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1094">Speech commands are not working as expected.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1095">若要使用语音命令，你的电脑上的语音和语言设置必须设置为 [Windows Mixed Reality 中支持的语言](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039262/windows-10-mixed-reality-setup-faq#Languages)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1095">To use speech commands, speech and language settings on your PC must be set to a [language supported in Windows Mixed Reality](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039262/windows-10-mixed-reality-setup-faq#Languages).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1096">若要检查您的 Windows 语音和语言设置，请选择 " **设置" > time & language > 区域 & 语言** 和 **设置 > time & language > 语音** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1096">To check your Windows speech and language settings, select **Settings  > Time & language > Region & language** and **Settings  > Time & language > Speech** .</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1097">如果耳机没有内置麦克风，则需要使用麦克风将耳机连接到耳机或电脑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1097">If your headset doesn’t have a built-in microphone, you’ll need to attach headphones with a microphone to the headset or to your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1098">要使麦克风输入在您磨损时自动切换到你的耳机，请转到 " **设置" > 混合现实 > 音频和语音** ，并打开 "当我戴上耳机时，切换到耳机麦克风"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1098">To have microphone input switch automatically to your headset when you wear it, go to **Settings > Mixed reality > Audio and speech** , and turn on "When I wear my headset, switch to headset mic".</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1099">某些音频耳机有一个 "物理" 按钮，可将麦克风静音并取消静音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1099">Some audio headsets have a physical button to mute and unmute the microphone.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1100">如果语音命令不起作用，请检查是否已将麦克风静音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1100">If speech commands aren't working, check to see whether your microphone is muted.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1101">带有麦克风的音频耳机，dangles 从 earbud 电缆连接时，不能很好地在环境干扰的环境中执行语音命令。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1101">Audio headsets with a microphone that dangles from the earbud cable do not perform well for voice commands in environments with ambient noise.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1102">首次在混合现实门户会话中调用 Cortana 时，Cortana 可能会很慢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1102">Cortana can be slow the first time she is invoked in a Mixed Reality Portal session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1103">请参阅 " **设置" > cortana > 与 Cortana 交谈** ，并确保已启用 "允许 Cortana 响应你好 cortana"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1103">Go to **Settings > Cortana > Talk to Cortana** and make sure "Let Cortana respond to Hey Cortana" is enabled.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1104">在某些电脑上，手机网络连接麦克风的默认语音捕获增益可能会设置得太低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1104">On some PCs, the default voice capture gain for your headset-connected microphone may be set too low.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1105">如果遇到不可靠的语音命令或听写，可以尝试运行麦克风安装疑难解答。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1105">If you experience unreliable speech commands or dictation, you can try running the Microphone Setup troubleshooter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1106">您可以通过 " **设置" > Time & Language > 语音** "来访问此疑难解答，然后在" 麦克风 "部分选择" 入门 "。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1106">You can reach this troubleshooter through the **Settings > Time & Language > Speech** , then select "Get Started" in the "Microphone" section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1107">通过桌面应用在 Windows Mixed Reality 主页中完成此操作，同时戴上耳机，影响用于 Windows Mixed Reality 的麦克风。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1107">Do this through the Desktop app in the Windows Mixed Reality home while wearing the headset to affect the microphone you use for Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1108">选择疑难解答向导中的相应终结点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1108">Select the appropriate endpoint in the troubleshooter wizard.</span></span>

### <a name="i-only-have-one-audio-headset-and-i-want-to-use-it-for-both-desktop-and-my-headset"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1109">我只有一个音频耳机，并想要将其用于桌面和耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1109">I only have one audio headset and I want to use it for both Desktop and my headset.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1110">如果只有一个音频耳机并且没有内置耳机的耳机，请将音频耳机连接到主机 PC 而不是耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1110">If you only have one audio headset and do not have a headset with built in headphones, connect the audio headset to the host PC instead of the headset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1111">然后关闭 MRP 设置中的 "切换到耳机音频"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1111">Then turn off "switch to headset audio" in the MRP settings.</span></span>

### <a name="i-want-to-switch-to-dolby-atmos-for-headphones"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1112">我要切换到杜比 Atmos 来寻找耳机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1112">I want to switch to Dolby Atmos for Headphones.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1113">Windows Mixed Reality 环境及其应用程序使用 Windows Sonic 实现耳机空间音频技术，该技术是为混合现实体验定制的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1113">Windows Mixed Reality environments and its applications use Windows Sonic for Headphones spatial audio technology which is customized for mixed reality experiences.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1114">其他空间音频技术（如耳机的杜比 Atmos）可应用于全屏应用程序（如 SteamVR 游戏，但不适用于 Windows Mixed Reality shell 环境和应用程序 (例如，将 web 浏览器放置在 Cliff 房子的墙壁上，或在天空 Loft) 使用 Windows Sonic 实现耳机空间音效和噪音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1114">Other spatial audio technologies, like Dolby Atmos for Headphones, can be applied for full screen applications like SteamVR games but not for the Windows Mixed Reality shell environments and applications (such as placing a web browser on the wall of the Cliff House or the Sky Loft) which have been designed using Windows Sonic for Headphones spatial sound and acoustics.</span></span>


## <a name="questions-about-desktop-in-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1115">有关混合现实中的桌面的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1115">Questions about Desktop in Mixed Reality</span></span>

### <a name="how-do-i-access-my-pc-desktop-in-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1116">如何实现在混合现实中访问我的 PC 桌面？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1116">How do I access my PC desktop in Mixed Reality?</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="79562-1117">您可以使用桌面应用程序访问混合现实中的 PC 桌面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1117">You can access your PC desktop in Mixed Reality using the Desktop app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1118">从 Windows 的 "耳机" **按钮启动 > 所有应用 > 桌面** "。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1118">Launch it in the headset from **Windows Button > All apps > Desktop** .</span></span> 

### <a name="how-can-i-see-multiple-monitors-in-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1119">如何在混合现实中查看多个监视器？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1119">How can I see multiple monitors in Mixed Reality?</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="79562-1120">默认情况下，桌面应用会自动切换为显示具有焦点的监视器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1120">By default, Desktop app automatically switches to display the monitor with focus.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1121">如果要在混合现实中查看所有监视器：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1121">If you want to see all of your monitors in Mixed Reality:</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1122">单击应用左上角的 "监视" 图标</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1122">Click the monitor icon on the top left corner of the app</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1123">禁用 "自动切换监视器"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1123">Disable "Automatically Switch Monitor"</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1124">选择要查看的监视器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1124">Pick the monitor you want to see</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1125">启动桌面应用程序的另一个实例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1125">Launch another instance of the Desktop app</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1126">选择要在该实例上查看的监视器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1126">Pick the monitor you want to see on that instance</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1127">对于所有物理监视器重复此操作，请注意，每次重新启动混合现实时，都必须重新选择要在每个桌面应用上显示的监视器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1127">Repeat for all of your physical monitors Note that you will have to reselect the monitor to show on each Desktop app every time you restart Mixed Reality.</span></span> 

### <a name="my-desktop-app-only-shows-a-black-screen"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1128">我的桌面应用程序只显示黑屏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1128">My Desktop app only shows a black screen.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="79562-1129">如果你的电脑具有 Nvidia 混合 GPU，则问题可能是由于 Nvidia 设备在离散 GPU 而不是集成的 GPU 上运行 runtimebroker.exe。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1129">If your PC has an Nvidia hybrid GPU, the issue may be caused by Nvidia device running the runtimebroker.exe on the discrete GPU instead of the integrated one.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1130">若要解决此问题，请按照 "[如何实现创建新程序的 Optimus 设置](http://nvidia.custhelp.com/app/answers/detail/a_id/2615/~/how-do-i-customize-optimus-profiles-and-settings%3F)" 下的说明操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1130">To fix this issue, follow these instructions under "[How do I create Optimus settings for a new program?](http://nvidia.custhelp.com/app/answers/detail/a_id/2615/~/how-do-i-customize-optimus-profiles-and-settings%3F)"</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1131">添加 C:\windows\system32\runtimebroker.exe，并强制其在 "集成图形" 处理器上运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1131">to add C:\windows\system32\runtimebroker.exe and force it to run on the "Integrated graphics" processor.</span></span> 


## <a name="other-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1132">其他问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1132">Other Questions</span></span>

### <a name="my-samsung-odyssey-or-odyssey-headset-firmware-update-is-getting-stuck"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1133">我的 Samsung 太空或太空 + 耳机固件更新堵塞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1133">My Samsung Odyssey or Odyssey+ headset firmware update is getting stuck.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1134">Samsung 拥有并发布通过其 "Samsung HMD 太空安装程序" 和 "Samsung HMD 太空 + Setup" 设备配套应用交付的耳机固件更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1134">Samsung owns and publishes headset firmware updates delivered via their "Samsung HMD Odyssey Setup" and "Samsung HMD Odyssey+ Setup" Device Companion apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1135">若要获得更多详细信息并了解 Samsung 固件更新问题，请联系 Samsung 客户服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1135">For more details and for help with Samsung firmware update issues, please reach out to Samsung Customer Service.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1136">如果固件更新过程停滞，而且没有进展超过五分钟：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1136">If the firmware update process is getting stuck, and there has been no progress for more than five minutes:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1137">暂时拔出所有其他 USB 设备，然后重试固件更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1137">Unplug all of your other USB devices temporarily and retry the firmware update.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1138">将 Samsung 耳机连接到电脑上的其他 USB 3.0 端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1138">Connect your Samsung headset to a different USB 3.0 port on your PC.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1139">禁用和/或卸载任何可能会干扰固件更新的软件，例如千兆 AORUS App Center。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1139">Disabling and/or uninstall any software installed that may interfere with firmware updates, like Gigabyte's AORUS App Center.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1140">使用其他 PC 来执行 Samsung 耳机固件更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1140">Use a different PC to perform the Samsung headset firmware update.</span></span>

### <a name="my-wi-fi-slows-down-when-im-using-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1141">使用 Windows Mixed Reality 时，Wi-fi 会变慢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1141">My Wi-Fi slows down when I'm using Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1142">如果使用的是 2.4 GHz Wi-fi 连接，则运动控制器可能会减慢 Wi-fi 的速度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1142">If you're using a 2.4GHz Wi-Fi connection, your motion controllers might slow down your Wi-Fi.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1143">尝试以下任一项：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1143">Try one of the following:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1144">切换到 5GHz Wi-fi 连接（如果有）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1144">Switch to a 5GHz Wi-Fi connection, if one is available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1145">[了解详细信息](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4000461)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1145">[Learn more](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4000461).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1146">使用单独的蓝牙适配器将运动控制器连接到您的 PC。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1146">Use a separate Bluetooth adapter to connect your motion controllers to your PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1147">请参阅 [建议的适配器](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1147">See [recommended adapters](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4039260/windows-10-mixed-reality-pc-hardware-guidelines).</span></span>

### <a name="i-got-a-message-that-said-to-plug-in-and-charge-my-pc-why"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1148">我收到一条消息，指出我的 PC 已接通电源并向其收费。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1148">I got a message that said to plug in and charge my PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1149">为什么？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1149">Why?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1150">如果使用便携式计算机，则当电脑完全充电并接通电源时，Windows Mixed Reality 的效果最佳。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1150">If you're using a laptop, Windows Mixed Reality works best when the PC is both fully charged and plugged in.</span></span> 

### <a name="what-is-the-experience-options-setting"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1151">什么是体验选项设置？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1151">What is the Experience options setting?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1152">体验选项将 ( **设置 > 混合现实 > 耳机显示 > 体验) 选项** ，使你可以更改 Windows Mixed reality 性能设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1152">The Experience options setting ( **Settings > Mixed reality > Headset display > Experience options** ) allows you to change the Windows Mixed Reality performance settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1153">这使你能够在一系列内容中为你的硬件配置选择可能的最佳体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1153">This enables you to choose the best possible experience for your hardware configuration across a range of content.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1154">90Hz 体验适用于所有系统，但你可能希望尝试自动查看所需的设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1154">The 90Hz experience is available to all systems, but you might want to try Automatic to see which setting you prefer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1155">选项如下：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1155">Here are the options:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1156">自动： Windows Mixed Reality 将确定硬件配置的最佳体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1156">Automatic: Windows Mixed Reality will determine the best experience for your hardware configuration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1157">对于大多数人来说，这是开始的最佳选择。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1157">For most people, this is the best choice to start with.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1158">60Hz：将刷新率设置为60Hz，并关闭某些功能，如混合现实门户中的视频捕获和预览。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1158">60Hz: Sets the refresh rate to 60Hz and turns off certain features, such as video capture and preview in Mixed Reality Portal.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79562-1159">90Hz：将刷新率设置为90Hz。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1159">90Hz: Sets the refresh rate to 90Hz.</span></span>
