## <a name="how-to-uninstall-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1186">如何卸载 Windows Mixed Reality</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1186">How to uninstall Windows Mixed Reality</span></span>

### <a name="how-do-i-uninstall-windows-mixed-reality"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1187">如何实现卸载 Windows Mixed Reality？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1187">How do I uninstall Windows Mixed Reality?</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1188">断开耳机与电脑的连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1188">Disconnect your headset from your PC.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1189">关闭混合现实门户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1189">Close Mixed Reality Portal.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1190">请参阅  **开始 > 设置 > Mixed Reality** ，然后选择 "卸载"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1190">Go to  **Start > Settings > Mixed Reality** and select "Uninstall".</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1191">如果已准备好开始使用头戴显示，请将其插入，混合现实门户将引导你完成安装过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1191">When you're ready to start using your headset again, plug it in, and Mixed Reality Portal will take you through setup.</span></span>

### <a name="i-got-a-we-couldnt-finish-uninstalling-windows-mixed-reality-message"></a><span data-ttu-id="79562-1192">我收到了 "我们无法完成 Windows Mixed Reality 的卸载" 消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1192">I got a "We couldn't finish uninstalling Windows Mixed Reality" message.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1193">这意味着，某些文件（包括有关您的环境的信息）可能仍在您的计算机上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1193">This means that some files, including information about your environment, might still be on your computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1194">如果你决定稍后重新安装 Windows Mixed Reality，这可能会导致问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1194">This can cause problems if you decide to reinstall Windows Mixed Reality later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1195">你可以通过修改注册表并使用 Windows PowerShell 来运行命令，从你的电脑中手动删除任何剩余的 Windows Mixed Reality 信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1195">You can manually remove any remaining Windows Mixed Reality info from your PC by modifying the registry and using Windows PowerShell to run commands.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1196">_如果不正确地修改注册表，则可能会出现严重问题。请确保仔细执行这些步骤。为了增加保护，请在修改注册表之前对其进行备份，以便在发生问题时可以还原。_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1196">_If you modify the registry incorrectly, serious problems might occur. Make sure to follow these steps carefully. For added protection, back up your registry before you modify it so you can restore it if a problem occurrs._</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1197">有关详细信息，请参阅 [如何在 Windows 中备份和 restory 注册表](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/322756/how-to-back-up-and-restore-the-registry-in-windows)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1197">For more info, see [How to back up and restory the registry in Windows](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/322756/how-to-back-up-and-restore-the-registry-in-windows).</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1198">使用以下命令卸载 Windows mixed reality：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1198">To uninstall Windows mixed reality using these commands:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1199">重启你的电脑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1199">Restart your PC.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1200">在 **搜索** 框中，键入 "regedit"，然后选择 **"是** "。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1200">In the **Search** box, type "regedit" and then select **Yes** .</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="79562-1201">删除以下注册表值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1201">Remove the following registry values:</span></span>
   <ul>
    <li><span data-ttu-id="79562-1202"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER \software\microsoft\windows\currentversion\holographic</b>，然后删除 <b>FirstRunSucceeded</b>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1202"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Holographic</b>, then delete <b>FirstRunSucceeded</b>.</span></span></li> 
    <li><span data-ttu-id="79562-1203"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER \software\microsoft\windows\currentversion\holographic\speechandaudio</b>，然后删除 <b>PreferDesktopSpeaker</b> 和 <b>PreferDesktopMic</b>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1203"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Holographic\SpeechAndAudio</b>, then delete <b>PreferDesktopSpeaker</b> and <b>PreferDesktopMic</b>.</span></span></li> 
    <li><span data-ttu-id="79562-1204"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER \software\microsoft\ Speech_OneCore &gt; Settings\Holographic</b>，然后删除 <b>DisableSpeechInput</b>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1204"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Speech_OneCore&gt; Settings\Holographic</b>, then delete <b>DisableSpeechInput</b>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79562-1205">注意：必须在已使用 Windows Mixed Reality 的 PC 上为每个用户帐户删除 HHKEY_CURRENT_USER 中的注册表项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1205">Note:the registry items in HHKEY_CURRENT_USER must be deleted for every user account on the PC that has used Windows Mixed Reality.</span></span></li> 
    <li><span data-ttu-id="79562-1206"><b>HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE \software\microsoft\windows\currentversion\perceptionsimulationextensions</b>，然后删除 <b>DeviceID</b> 和 <b>Mode</b>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1206"><b>HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\PerceptionSimulationExtensions</b>, then delete <b>DeviceID</b> and <b>Mode</b>.</span></span></li> 
    <li><span data-ttu-id="79562-1207"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER \software\microsoft\windows\currentversion\holographic</b>，然后删除 <b>OnDeviceLearningCompleted</b>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1207"><b>HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Holographic</b>, then delete <b>OnDeviceLearningCompleted</b>.</span></span></li> 
   </ul><span data-ttu-id="79562-1208">

<span data-ttu-id="79562-1213">6. 导航到 **C:\users\ 用户名 name\appdata\local\packages\ Microsoft.Windows.HolographicFirstRun_cw5n1h2txyewy \localstate** ，然后删除 **RoomBounds.json** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79562-1213">6.
